Educational Circles in Beiping Request that Beiping Be Designated as a City of Culture

Listing Reasons to Preserve Culture; All Military Equipment Moved to Baoding

Hoping that Beiping Will Become Like Switzerland

Beiping Correspondence: Jiang Han, Liu Fu, Xu Bingchang, Ma Heng, Zhu Qizhao and more than 30 people from the educational circles in Beiping, given that the stationed troops in Beiping, should accidents occur in the future, the relics stored will suffer huge losses, held a meeting on the 21st of last month to discuss. It was decided to propose to the government to designate Beiping as a city of culture, remove military equipment, and Liu Fu drafted a statement of opinion, which was publicly recommended by Jiang Han to petition the government. It has now been decided that Ma Heng will represent them in Nanjing to discuss the matter. Ma left Beiping southward at 5 PM on the 5th, planning to contact all parties first after arriving in Nanjing, state his opinions, and formally submit the statement of opinion to the government on Double Tenth Day. The original text of the statement of opinion is copied as follows:

Beiping, this place, analyzed by nature, is a collection of political, military, and cultural regions. Before June of the 17th year of the Republic of China, Beijing was the capital of China and the first political region in the country. Later, the capital was moved south, and Beiping lost its importance in Chinese politics. Although a Political Affairs Committee is still set up, it is the political center of North China. Thoroughly speaking, this Political Affairs Committee is not necessary to be set up in Beiping. For the convenience of transportation, Tianjin is better than Beiping. The reason why it is set up in Beiping is only because there are vacant houses that can be borrowed, plus the general public's nostalgia for Beiping's importance in past political history, so it is still recognized as a secondary political region. In order to follow suit, Beiping's military region followed the political region. In the past, since the central government was located here, it should naturally have corresponding military facilities, the so-called "guarding the capital" is necessary both in fact and in the national system. However, Beiping itself is an open place and cannot be set up as a fortress, and has no military importance. In the fourth year of the Republic of China, when Japan proposed the Twenty-One Demands, the Beijing government ordered the General Staff Headquarters to jointly invite Chinese and foreign military experts from the Ministry of the Army and Navy to hold a national defense conference, and the experts went to inspect places such as Gubeikou and Nankou in person. The results showed that once there was a conflict between China and Japan, excluding the three eastern provinces and the coastal provinces, focusing on North China, the first defense line should be at Shanhaiguan. If Shanhaiguan cannot be defended, Tianjin and Beiping will definitely not be able to be defended. Therefore, the important town in North China should be Baoding, with Chengde in Rehe and Zhangjiakou in Chahar as secondary points. Beiping's ability to be a cultural region naturally followed the political region. If Beiping had not been able to serve as the capital of China for the past few hundred years, and had not been able to concentrate the talents and economy of the whole of China in one place, and managed it extremely well, I am afraid that today's Beiping would be no more than a county town like other ordinary counties in Hebei, or at most just like Baoding. Now the question we want to study is this: Beiping's political region has now reached a point where it is insignificant. Should its military and cultural regions still coexist in parallel, or should there be a focus? In our opinion, the military region and the cultural region cannot coexist in one place. A place that is a military region must prepare for war, while a cultural region cannot withstand war. Therefore, to focus on military affairs, all cultural facilities must be moved away. Then, which one should be moved away? Let us calmly study it.

First, as mentioned earlier, Beiping's political region has reached a point where it is insignificant. That is to say, it is okay to set it up in Beiping or not to set it up in Beiping. Even if it is set up in Beiping, it is different from the previous central government, and there is no need to set up troops to guard it.

Second, although Beiping is said to be a military region, in fact, there are no fixed military facilities, only some troops are stationed, and these troops are not fixed, and they are not specially trained to defend Beiping or maintain Beiping's security. They are only the guards of the actual rulers, and the strength of these rulers is not in the troops in Beiping City. When other aspects of the road are impassable, although Beiping still has some troops, they are useless. This can be proved by past facts.

Third, Beiping itself has no military importance, as mentioned earlier. Moreover, with the increasingly severe air warfare now, before a formal conflict, the enemy will first use aircraft to bomb our rear headquarters and various warehouses to shake the morale of the army. From this point of view, Beiping's target is too big. Therefore, setting up a military region in Beiping is not only not beneficial to national defense, but also harmful.

Fourth, it is difficult to collect cultural items, but it is very easy to lose them. The important reasons for the loss are war and relocation.

Fifth, cultural buildings cannot be moved.

Sixth, because Beiping has various cultural facilities, most of the specialized scholars of various disciplines in the country gather in Beiping, creating a cultural atmosphere that represents national civilization and earns honor for the country internationally. This atmosphere cannot be cultivated overnight. Once all the cultural facilities in Beiping are moved away, these scholars will inevitably disperse. To create such a cultural atmosphere again elsewhere is probably not an easy task.

Based on the above six reasons, the first three explain that moving the military equipment from Beiping is beneficial and harmless to national defense, and there is no practical difficulty. The latter three explain that if the cultural equipment of Beiping is to be moved away, it is not only impossible in practice, but also tantamount to reducing the cultural atmosphere that has been cultivated for hundreds of years. Therefore, we advocate requesting the government to designate Beiping as a city of culture and move all military equipment to Baoding. The police will be fully responsible for the security of Beiping. The responsibility for maintaining local security has always been shared by both the military and the police. In fact, the police force is probably the majority, and the army is only in a very weak supporting position. Our purpose is to reduce the possibility of Beiping's cultural facilities being hit by artillery fire. Of course, the enemy's morality should be considered. Perhaps we will remove the military equipment, and the enemy will still create all kinds of false accusations in order to destroy Beiping's culture. We naturally have no way to think about this, but Beiping is the seat of foreign envoys, and we may as well assume that there is not such a great and barbaric nation in the world that dares to destroy cultural facilities that have no resistance under the public gaze. Therefore, we can first do our best. All the cultural items in Beiping, such as the Stone Drums collected by Confucius, the Yin Shang oracle bones collected by the Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica, the Han Dynasty wooden slips excavated by the Northwest Science Expedition, the Yuan Dynasty murals in the Peking University, the Siku Quanshu, Dunhuang scriptures, and other rare books collected by the Beiping Library, and the Chao Dynasty's national music for offering sacrifices to heaven collected in the Temple of Heaven, are all treasures with unparalleled value in Chinese cultural history, and even in world cultural history, and can be called national treasures. As for the architecture and treasures of the Forbidden City and the Ancient Artifacts Exhibition Hall, they are especially admired by museums all over the world. Even though the instruments of various universities and research institutes are not as good as those of foreign universities, they are much more complete than those of other universities and research institutes in the country. These things, to put it lightly, are enough to promote national glory, and to put it deeply, they are the place where the national lifeline and national spirit are entrusted. Their importance does not lie in the amount of money they are worth, but in the fact that most of them cannot be purchased after they are destroyed, and the value of money cannot be calculated. Although everyone in our country has the determination to sacrifice, the cultural items that promote national glory, entrust the national lifeline, and the national spirit must not be sacrificed. If these things are sacrificed, what exactly are we fighting for when we sacrifice everything? We hope that the future Beiping will be like Switzerland in Europe, never invaded by war, and like Oxford and Cambridge in England, always immersed in the clear spring of culture. We hope that the government will accept our request, and we hope that the military authorities with broad vision will earnestly support us. We hope that the politicians and activists of all countries in the world who love peace and culture will give us appropriate help to prove everything. (6th)

Journey to the West (3) (10) (5)

Ways to Exploit Shaanxi Coal

After geologist Mr. Huang Boda completed his investigation of the northern Shaanxi coalfields, he had the following opinions on the ways to exploit Shaanxi coal:

I (Mr. Huang referring to himself), representing the China Mining Society, participated in the Shaanxi Industrial Investigation Group this time. I traveled through more than ten counties, covering a distance of more than two thousand miles. The general situation and opinions are briefly described as follows: (1) The mines investigated include the Xincun Gou, Hui Tui Po, Bai Gong Miao, and Chenjia River mines in Tongguan County; the Yaoxian Village in Yijun County; the Jia Gou, Zhangjia Gou, Qilizhen, and Houziping mines; and the Zhuyuan, Shijia Gou, Quan Yu Gou, Er Gou, and Xi Gou mines in Hancheng County. (2) Coal price survey: The coal price in the Xi'an area is surprisingly high. The coal price in Xi'an is about more than forty yuan per ton. According to the Construction Department, the highest price was once two hundred yuan per ton. The coal prices in other counties are listed as follows:

Xi'an 44.2 yuan Tongguan 10.2 yuan

Xianyang 44.2 yuan Fushi 10.2 yuan

Sanyuan 24.65 yuan Yanchang 11.9 yuan

Yaoxian 8.5 yuan Yichuan 28.9 yuan

Yijun 8.5 yuan Gancheng 10.2 yuan

中部 (中部) 9.35 yuan Taiyang 14 yuan

Luochuan 11.9 yuan

(3) Estimated coal reserves: According to general estimates, calculating the coal seam thickness at 4, 5, or 6 meters seems overly optimistic. In this survey, the Yijun coal seam thickness varied from 4 feet to 8 feet, with an average of 2 meters. The Tongguan coal seam thickness varied from 6 feet to 8 feet, with an average of 2 meters. The Hancheng coal seam thickness can be calculated at 1.6 meters. However, due to the brief nature of the visit, the strike, dip, and extent of each coalfield could not be measured. The following is a summary of the estimated coal reserves based on Mr. Qu Guobin's records:

(A) Yijun coalfield: Approximately 40,000 meters long from north to south and approximately 3,000 meters wide from east to west, with a coal seam thickness of approximately 2 meters. Assuming a specific gravity of 1, the coal reserves should be 240 million tons. (B) Tongguan coalfield: Approximately 72,000 meters long and approximately 4,800 meters wide, with a varying coal seam thickness. Using 2 meters for calculation and assuming a specific gravity of 1, the coal reserves should be approximately 340 million tons. (C) Hancheng coalfield: Approximately 6,000 meters long and approximately 12,000 meters wide, with a coal seam thickness of 1.6 meters and a specific gravity of 1, the coal reserves should be approximately 115 million tons. The total coal reserves in the above three locations are approximately 173 million tons. (D) The Jurassic coal seams in counties such as Yao County, Fushi, and Yanchang are about 2 feet thick. Local people use primitive mining methods and are still able to profit. Any mine that can be profitably extracted from the ground and sold in the market has exploitation value. Therefore, the coal in counties such as Yao County, Fushi, and Yanchang should not be considered absolutely worthless. The coal reserves could not be estimated due to the unknown length and width.

(4) Reasons for high coal prices: The high coal prices in Xi'an and other places are purely due to transportation difficulties, not to particularly high coal mining costs. The selling price of coal in the mining areas is about two yuan per ton, such as in Hancheng and Yijun. The highest is no more than four yuan, such as in Chenjia River, Tongguan. The coal mining cost in Tongguan is about two yuan, and in Yijun and Hancheng it is about one to two yuan. It is clear that the coal mining cost is not particularly high. The biggest difficulty is transportation. Most coal-producing areas are mountainous and rely on animals for transportation. Hancheng Coal Mine also uses the Yellow River to transport coal. The situation is briefly described as follows: (A) From the mine to Wanmenkou, a distance of 15 li, manual transportation costs 2.8 yuan per ton (4 jiao per 240 jin). From Yu Menkou to Di Kai Shui by water, 8.4 yuan per ton (1.2 yuan per 240 jin). The total transportation cost from the mine to Huguan is 11.2 yuan per ton. (B) From the mine to Ping Yu Menkou, manual transportation costs 2.8 yuan per ton. From Yu Menkou to Baiyangzhai, water transport costs 12.6 yuan per ton. From Baiyangzhai to Xi'an, manual transportation costs 16.8 yuan per ton. The total transportation cost from the mine to Xi'an is 32.2 yuan. From this, it can be seen that the failure to develop the northern Shaanxi coalfields is purely a transportation problem, not excessive coal mining costs.

(5) Development Approaches: The Shaanxi Basin produces coal in both the center and the edges. The Jurassic coal seams are in the center of the basin. The thickness of the coal seams varies greatly, and there are many intermediate strata, so the ash content is particularly high and the sulfur content is also heavy, as in the Yijun coal mine. The Carboniferous-Permian coal seams are on the edge of the basin. The average thickness of the coal seams is about 2 meters, and the coal quality is quite good. The rocks above and below the coal seams are sandstone, and there is very little need for timber supports, as in Tongguan and Hancheng. If you want to develop the Shaanxi coalfields, it seems more advantageous to start with the Tongguan and Hancheng coal mines. Hancheng is 245 li from Tongguan, and can be sold overseas via the sea route. It is about 270-280 li from Qunxian. The area already has an arsenal. If Huayin is established as an industrial zone, the coal consumption will be significant. Along the way, counties such as Taiyang, Dali, and Chaoyi consume about 100,000 shun of coal per year. In the future, high-altitude light rail should be built for transportation in mountainous areas, and light rails can be built on flat ground. Tongguan is 245 li from Xianyang. Xianyang is a planned route for the sea route and can be transported outwards. If Xianyang is established as an industrial zone, it can also consume a large amount of coal. However, transporting and selling coal eastward from Xianyang requires an additional one yuan per ton. The transportation cost for importing raw materials and exporting products eastward will also be higher than in Huayin. Therefore, I believe that it would be more convenient to establish an industrial zone in Huayin than in Xianyang. If Huayin is designated as an industrial expense area, then the development of the Gancheng coalfield should be prioritized over Tongguan. The large-scale mining of coal seams and the method of transportation still require further research. Some advocate using the Yellow River for transportation, but the Yellow River's riverbed changes unpredictably and the transportation cost is surprisingly high, so it does not seem to have any exploitation value. (Sent from Taiyang on September 13)

The Mid-Autumn Festival Without Moonlight

Heaven seems to be as fickle as a woman. On the morning of the 13th,

Page 10

just as we were about to depart from Taiyang, it started raining again. At 7 o'clock, we ate in the drizzling rain. From 8 to 10 o'clock, we exchanged opinions with local people from all walks of life in Taiyang. From 10 to 12 o'clock, we all attended a welcoming party. At about 1 o'clock in the afternoon, after lunch, we set off for Lujing Town with our rain gear.

That day's journey was only 40 li. Those of us on horseback arrived in two hours. By then, the rain had stopped, but the sky was covered with dark clouds. Heaven still had a long face, as if it had something unpleasant to vent. Although Lujing Town is a town, it has solid city walls on all sides, and there are several shops in the city. The scale is comparable to that of a small county. That night, we looked up, but could not find the bright moon of the approaching Mid-Autumn Festival in the dark sky. Originally, the Mid-Autumn moon is exceptionally bright. Who stole the joy of this year's moon goddess, hiding her bright and beautiful face, so that she could not meet our lonely travelers!

On the morning of the 14th, the sky was still covered with rain, and the cold north wind blew against our backs, making us feel not only that the cool autumn of September was coming to an end, but also that the severe winter was approaching step by step. At 11 o'clock, we arrived at Fangquan Town from Lujing Town. Many people in the town died in the past due to the rampant tiger plague. While we were resting and eating, we saw swarms of flies, like black clouds, landing on the food. It is truly impossible to prevent the tiger plague from raging. By then, the rain had stopped and the weather had warmed up a little. Those of us on horseback, at about 12:30, rushed forward desperately, completing the 40-li journey in two hours, and arriving at our last investigation area, Dali County.

Dali is the former Tongzhou. The market is very prosperous. Every month on the 3rd, 7th, etc., is the period of commercial gatherings, and the three days of the Mid-Autumn Festival, the 14th, 15th, and 16th, are the busiest sales period of the year. When we entered the city, we saw a sea of people in the streets, and tiny-footed rebellious women walking in the streets with delicate steps, almost making us doubt that the 18th century was about to be resurrected. According to local people, the area of the county is about more than 6,000 hectares, the circumference of the city is about 9 li, it is slightly longer east-west and narrower north-south, the population of the county is about 100,000, the city has about 12,000 people, and there are about 200-300 shops. When I arrived at my accommodation, I met Li Yuhua, the director of the Education Bureau, Li Baoqing, the director of the Finance Bureau, and Gao Tianmin, the director of the Construction Bureau.

They provided me with a lot of information. The statistics of various specialties are roughly as follows:

As for education, there are 5 complete elementary schools, 5 junior elementary schools, 11 people's schools, a vocational supplementary school, a girls' elementary school, and a people's education center. The education expenditure of the Education Bureau is about 4,320 yuan per year, 3,000 yuan for the First Elementary School, 560 yuan for the Second Elementary School, 840 yuan for the Third Elementary School, 720 yuan for the Fourth Elementary School, 540 yuan for the Fifth Elementary School, 2,520 yuan for the Vocational Supplementary School, 2,160 yuan for the Girls' Elementary School, 444 yuan for the Model Junior Elementary School, 252 yuan for the First Junior Elementary School, 228 yuan for the Second Junior Elementary School, 22 yuan for the Third Junior Elementary School, 252 yuan for the Fourth Junior Elementary School, 720 yuan for the People's Education Center, and 160 yuan for each People's School. The salaries of the staff are 30 yuan per month for the director of the Education Bureau, 20 yuan for the principal, 20 yuan for the director of the Education Fund Management Office, 17 yuan for the document clerk, 15 yuan for the secretary, 17 yuan for the office worker, 15 yuan for the education commissioner, 24 yuan for the principal, 22 yuan for the director of studies, 20 yuan for the senior homeroom teacher, 18 yuan for the junior homeroom teacher, and 20 yuan for the director of the People's Education Center. Local Communications

Songjiang

Reconvening the Millennium Gathering: The elderly people in this county, aged 60 and above, once gathered to form the Millennium Gathering. They held two general meetings every year, feasting and celebrating at famous scenic spots. This spring, due to the Shanghai war, it was not held. Now, elders such as Geng Boqi, Xiao Yuan, and Cai Zhongyu believe that it is very appropriate to continue the 30th Autumn Gathering in this clear and refreshing autumn. They have decided to hold a meeting at the Fire Brigade Association on the 15th of this month, and have already informed elders from all over the region to attend on time. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Elementary School Teacher Suicide: Wang Guixiang, a teacher who used to work at the County Experimental Elementary School and is from Changzhou, committed suicide because he failed to find a job in Shanghai and was living in the Experimental School. The previous night, he had the idea of committing suicide. He bought sleeping pills and swallowed them secretly. Fortunately, his colleagues noticed that his expression was different and also knew that he had attempted suicide in the Wusong River several times without success. Therefore, he was immediately sent to Songjiang Hospital for treatment. It is said that he took a heavy dose and his life has not yet been saved.

Fengxian

Combined Collection of Land Survey and Mu Tax: The land survey and mu tax of this county were previously decided by the budget meeting of the 21st year to be suspended for one year, but the order was rejected by the department. As the first phase of land tax has already started, the county government has now obtained approval from the finance department to collect one jiao together with the second phase of land tax. As for the custody issue, it has also been reorganized in accordance with the newly promulgated regulations. In fact, of the amount collected, in addition to the more than 43,000 yuan received in the 15th and 20th years, there is still 30,000 yuan that has not been paid in full. Yesterday, Dong Jinzhao, the director in charge of the Land Bureau, sent a letter to the Finance Bureau requesting that it be paid off in full within ten days to supplement the funds.

Taicang

Autopsy in the Case of Wife Abuse Resulting in Death: Shi Zuoxiong, a resident of Dongmen Street in the city, married Huang. After marriage, due to the disparity in wealth, the couple was not harmonious. The other day, due to a trivial quarrel, he abused Huang to death and abandoned the body in the back river. The next morning, he claimed that she had committed suicide in the river. After the Huang's family reported to the county for an autopsy, on the morning of the 5th, Wu, the trial officer, came to the scene for inspection. It was found that the deceased had multiple bruises on her face and body, indicating that she had been beaten to death before her death. The body was handed over to the Huang's family for burial. Shi Zuoxiong was detained in the county and imprisoned for punishment.

Wuxi

Young Traveler Dies by Poison: At about 9 o'clock the previous evening, a young traveler arrived at the Railway Hotel under the Gongyun Bridge. He was wearing a dark blue-gray real wool jacket, a high-quality felt hat, and leather shoes. He did not bring any luggage. He claimed to be Feng Shiguang, from Shanghai, and 24 years old. He immediately booked room 52 upstairs and paid two yuan for the room. He then went out to a restaurant for a hearty drink, and returned to the inn to rest after 12 o'clock. Unexpectedly, at about 11 o'clock yesterday morning, the guest had not yet gotten up. When they called him, he did not respond. The waiter peeked through the door gap and saw Feng lying on the bed with his clothes on, his face pale, his mouth and eyes slightly open. He immediately reported to the accounting room. They pried open the door and found that he had been dead for a long time. After searching the room, there were no belongings, only a long, round empty bottle was found under the bed. At 2 o'clock in the afternoon, waiter Yang Fuquan, together with Tu Zheng Xi Zhiliang, reported to the county court for an autopsy. Prosecutor Shen, accompanied by two inspectors Wang and Jia, came to the scene for an autopsy and confirmed that he had died of poisoning. After the autopsy, he immediately ordered Tu Zheng to prepare a coffin and seal it up.

Sudden Labor Strike at Qian Shen Silk Factory: Yesterday afternoon, a sudden labor strike occurred at the Qian Shen Silk Factory under the Gongyun Bridge. In the morning, all the female workers came to the factory to work and there was nothing unusual. There was no movement even during the meal break. Unexpectedly, at 1 o'clock in the afternoon, when the factory blew the whistle to start work as usual, suddenly no female workers came to the factory. The workers who brought their meals to eat in the factory also left the factory one after another. Cheng Bingruo, the comprador of the factory, knew that there was a change and immediately ordered the car management staff to gather in the workshop. In an instant, the female workers gathered at the factory gate, shouting and making noise, saying that they needed to improve their treatment and increase their wages. At that time, the voices were noisy and the order was chaotic. Fearing that it would cause trouble, the factory immediately telegraphed the Public Security Second Branch in charge and sent police to suppress it. The County Public Security Bureau also sent horses to the scene to persuade the female workers. The factory immediately convened a factory affairs meeting to discuss follow-up measures, but as of the time of sending the letter, there was no concrete solution.

Changzhou

County Government Executes Two Bandits by Firing Squad: The two bandits Tang Dagou and Liu Fuxi, who were previously captured by the Wu Yi County Government, confessed to robbery and other cases after several trials. They were sentenced to death and submitted to the provincial government for approval to execute. At 6 o'clock on the morning of the 8th, County Magistrate Zhang Peng sent the police to bring the two criminals to the case to verify their identities and tie them to the execution ground to be shot.

Prosecution for Abuse Case: Yang Defang, a blacksmith in Dingyan Town, Wu Yi, and his wife Yang Zhang, treated their adopted daughter-in-law Wu Mei harshly, causing her serious injury and death. The County Court Prosecutor's Office took Yang Defang and his wife into custody based on the report and sent staff to open the coffin for an autopsy. It was confirmed that she had been beaten to death, which was unbearable to see. After several court hearings, they were prosecuted to the Criminal Court yesterday.

Danyang

Jailer Accused: Li Yingchang, the jailer and warden of this county, has been deeply resented by the prisoners in the prison since he took office. Recently, someone went to the Ministry and the Hospital to report him for raping female prisoners, deducting prisoners' food, and embezzling salaries. First, the Jiangsu Higher Court sent staff to Danyang to investigate. Yesterday (the 7th), the Ministry of Justice Administration also sent Zhao Gonglai to Danyang for a secret investigation. It has been found that the official forged invoices and falsely reported prices. He returned to the Ministry by car that night to report.

Robbery and Kidnapping Case in Xixiang: Yu Yingfu, a farmer in Matangwei Village, Xixiang, (on the 6th) was suddenly attacked by many bandits who searched and robbed his house separately. Before leaving, they kidnapped Xia Zijiugeng. The case has now been reported to the police for investigation.

Nantong

Sand Field Case Criminals Transferred to Court: The Nantong County Government, in accordance with provincial orders, arrested the main criminals Xu Xiaoxian in the case of damaging the educational sand dam. After interrogation, he admitted to the crimes of breaking the embankment and arson, and ordered him to confiscate 500 mu of the Xu's sand field. Xu Xiaoxian presented to the court, suing Nantong County for abusing its power and illegally arresting people, and requested salvation. On the 7th, the Nantong Court sent a bailiff Zhu Rushan to the County Government with a special protection order from the Higher Court to arrest Xu Xiaoxian for investigation and handling.

Ministry Sends Staff to Investigate Privately Installed Telephones: The Nantong Haimen Dongsan County long-distance telephone has not been approved by the Ministry of Communications. The Ministry believes that it encroaches on state-owned enterprises and ordered the three telegraph bureau directors to forcibly dismantle it together with the three county magistrates. However, the three county magistrates reported to the Ministry that the telephone was related to the joint defense military affairs of the three counties and requested that it be exempted from dismantling. Currently, the Ministry of Communications has sent Committee Member Huang to the territory to investigate the facts.

Rugao

Bandits in Zhoujiayuan Kill People: Huang Shiqiu, a wealthy household in Zhoujiayuan, Jiang'an District, was suddenly attacked by many bandits on the night of the 3rd. They searched and captured Huang, and shot him twice in the head, killing him on the spot. The next morning, the security regiment stationed near the regiment captured a bandit named Ding Yueqiu, who confessed that he committed the crime. He was presented to the general regiment headquarters for interrogation on the 4th.

Gaoyou

Lubaoxhuang Robbed Twice by Bandits: Lubaoxhuang, in the 6th District of the county, has about 40-50 households. On the 26th of last month, more than 30 bandits suddenly came with guns and searched house by house. As a result, they only got more than 30 yuan. The bandits came again the other day and brought four large boats. The bandits dispersed and robbed the rice from the farmers' homes, forcing Jiang Min to carry the rice to the boats. All the rice in the village was robbed, totaling more than 1,000 shi. When the bandits left the village, most of the farmers cried bitterly. Xinghua Police Team Rescues Hostages: Shi Decheng, the captain of the Xinghua police team, led his team to suppress bandits in the southwest of the county. They encountered a bandit boat with a large red flag of the "First Army of the World" hanging on it. Captain Shi immediately led the team to open fire and pursue the bandits. The bandits fled southwest. They chased to Puzheng, Youjing, and intercepted a bandit boat. There were seven hostages left on the boat. They were brought back to the Xinghua County Government for handling.

Yangzhou

Persuade Villagers to Carry Out Land Survey: The land survey storm in the Second District of Jiangdu has lasted for two weeks. Although it is now quiet, the land survey work should still be carried out. Since the province sent two companies of security troops to Yangzhou, stationed in various villages and towns to assist in the work, Yang County Magistrate and Director Zhong and the staff actively prepared for it. At 3 pm on the 7th, he convened more than 400 people, including the heads of villages and towns in the 2nd, 3rd, and 4th districts, and the directors of the Public Security Bureau, to hold a meeting in the county government auditorium. The county magistrate presided over the meeting and detailed that the land survey was to prevent the Zhoutou grain difference and fraud by the clerk, and the tax reform would enrich the national and local finances. Then, the heads of villages and towns in each district reported the situation of inciting the storm. The county magistrate advised the heads of villages and towns to work hard to persuade the villagers.

Please Preserve the Martyrs' Shrine: The Guangling Twelve Martyrs' Shrine was originally in the Fuxue of this city, dedicated to the martyrs who died for the country in the Yi You year of the Ming Dynasty. It is now known that the Ancient Relics Preservation Committee heard that the People's Education Center intends to demolish the shrine. Yesterday, they specifically requested the county government not to demolish it.

Qingjiang

Execution of a Large Number of Notorious Bandits: After the notorious bandits Jiang Xuejing and others, who were entrenched in the Huai Lian Si area, were captured by the garrison troops, they confessed to besieging Sankeshu, robbing Yugou, and burning and killing Wangjia Oil Mill and Lingqiao. After approval by Commander Chen Diaoyuan, on the morning of the 4th, except for Wu Fenghai, Lin Bi, Wang Houyuan, and Liu Chuanfang, who were taken to the town and shot at the request of the gentry of Yugou, the other eight people, including Jiang Xuejing, Cheng Weigang, Zhang Shaojing, Fang Xiaoyouzi, Wu Guoshu, Wu Yingcui, Ding Changnian, and Liu Qingyang, were shot at the execution ground at the root of the West City Wall.

Jiaxing

Provincial Order to Reduce the Number of Backbone Teams: The number of backbone teams in the Jiaxing County Security Regiment was originally set at 400. The county government believed that funds were not available, making it difficult to recruit them. Therefore, it specially submitted a request to the province for reduction. It has now been ordered that the county must recruit at least 200 of the quota and complete the recruitment by the deadline without delay.

Huzhou

Major Fire at Chao Yin Bridge on Nanjie: At about 4 pm yesterday (the 6th), a fire broke out in Yu Dachang's cotton shop on the north side of Chao Yin Bridge on Nanjie in this city. The fire spread to 12 shops, including Dachang's salted fish shop, Xue Yitai's tofu shop, and the meat shop and nail shop. It took two hours to extinguish the fire. It is reported that the loss from this fire is estimated to be more than 20,000 yuan in total.

Xiaoshan

Robbery Case in Daitang Township: More than 20 bandits suddenly came to the home of Jin Bangquan, a resident of Daitang Township outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan, on the night of the 5th and robbed all the clothes and silver dollars, totaling more than 700 yuan. The owner was not at home at the time. The bandits intended to set fire to the house, but fortunately, the female relatives begged and saved it. The county government sent staff to investigate and ordered the pursuit.

Ningbo

Conference on Bandit Suppression Settles on Measures

Zhao Cisheng, the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Seventh Special District of Eastern Zhejiang, convened a conference on bandit suppression at Zhixiang Hospital in Sheng County on the 7th. The results were as follows: (1) The bandit suppression methods will be drafted and implemented by Commander Zhang Jiechen. (2) Bandit suppression troops who capture three or more bandits will be awarded 300 yuan; five or more will be awarded 500 yuan; ten or more will be awarded 1,000 yuan; and so on. The funds will be raised by the county magistrate, and if there is a shortfall, the commissioner will be responsible for raising the funds to cover it. (3) Each county must have a certain number of detectives to act as eyes and ears for bandit suppression. (4) The Lianjia system must be implemented in accordance with the order from the provincial government, and the security team should cooperate with the landlords and administrative officials to expedite the expansion of the volunteer corps, and implement joint defense measures in accordance with the order. (6) The original detectives in Daishan will be expanded to sixty, and the expenses will be shared equally by six counties, including Fenghua, Shangyu, Yao, and Ci. The funds must be raised within one month and established as soon as possible. The required firearms and ammunition will be issued by Commander Zhang and Commissioner Zhao. The rest is omitted.

Shangyu

Verdict on Wife-Killing Case

Song Hehua, the wife of Zhu Wu-ba of Lisi, Shaoxing, had an affair with Shunlai, a cook at the Chunxing Restaurant in Baiguan. Zhu found out about this and stabbed Zhu to death on the morning of the 27th of last month. Afterwards, he took the murder weapon and rushed to the Third Public Security Bureau of Baiguan to surrender. The Third Public Security Bureau sent Zhu to the county government, and after repeated interrogations, he confessed without denial. Zhu Mao-shi, the mother of the deceased, also confirmed the facts. The county court recently sentenced him to death. However, it was found that after Zhu stabbed Hehua, he rushed to the Third Public Security Bureau to surrender himself, which is in accordance with the provisions of Article 38 of the same law, so the sentence for the primary crime should be reduced by one-third, and he is sentenced to eight years of imprisonment and deprivation of public rights for eight years. The number of days of detention before the judgment is allowed to be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The murder weapon, a knife, is confiscated.

Correspondence

Letter from the Construction Bureau of Changshu County

Dear Editor,

I have read a news item in the local communication column of your esteemed newspaper on the 3rd of this month, which stated that local people and various organizations in our county oppose the levy of additional land tax for water conservancy. I am extremely surprised. After investigation, it has been determined that the levy of additional land tax for water conservancy in our county last year was limited to one year. The funds collected were designated for local dredging of waterways and were not remitted to the province. The levy of this additional land tax has been discontinued this year. As of today, the Construction Department has not issued any orders to the county to continue the levy. How could local people and various organizations express opposition? The information reported in your newspaper is completely inconsistent with the facts. I am writing to request that you investigate and correct the report.

Respectfully,

The Head of the Affairs Section of the Construction Bureau of Changshu County,

October 7th

General Comparison of Elementary School Expenses in Jiangsu over the Past 20 Years

The Joint Office for the Preparation of Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province has compiled a general comparison of the expenditures of elementary schools in various counties from the first year to the twentieth year. The main points are excerpted below:

(1) The total expenditure of various counties in the first year was 1,389,894 yuan. It increased to 1,910,744 yuan in the fifth year, 2,504,999 yuan in the tenth year, 2,605,954 yuan in the fifteenth year, and 4,422,168 yuan in the twentieth year. Compared with the beginning, the total increase was 3,032,274 yuan, which is 3.23 times the expenditure in the first year.

(2) Among the total expenditures of each year, only the fifteenth year decreased by 245,481 yuan compared to the fourteenth year due to military affairs, and the nineteenth year decreased by 14,716 yuan compared to the eighteenth year due to the Provincial Department of Finance encroaching on local education funds. The remaining years all increased compared to the previous year.

(3) Comparing the total increased expenditure of each year, the years 3, 6, 10, 12, and 13 were each less than the increase of the previous year. The year with the largest increase in expenditure was the eighteenth year with 1,155,28 yuan, while the year with the smallest increase was the third year with 44,383 yuan. (4) Among the twenty years, the county with the most decreases in expenditure was County, which decreased in expenditure five times, and the least was once. Among them, the counties with the fewest decreases in expenditure were Jurong, Lishui, Zhenjiang, Changshu, Rugao, Baoshan, Kunshan, Funing, Yancheng, and Dongtai.

(5) In the twenty years, only in the eighth and ninth years did the expenditures of each county increase without decreasing. In other years, the increases and decreases in expenditures of each county were quite inconsistent, especially before the sixteenth year and in the nineteenth and twentieth years.

(6) Comparing the expenditures of each county every five years, there were ten counties in the fifth year whose expenditures decreased compared to the first year, fifteen counties in the tenth year whose expenditures decreased compared to the fifth year, seventeen counties in the fifteenth year whose expenditures decreased compared to the tenth year, and seven counties in the twentieth year whose expenditures decreased compared to the fifteenth year. (7) Although the total expenditure in the twentieth year increased by 3.23 times compared to the total expenditure in the first year, analyzing and comparing the expenditures of each county, the expenditures in the twentieth year were still less than those in the first year. In addition to Shanghai Municipality, which decreased by 33,056 yuan, Gaoyou decreased by 11,666 yuan due to floods, and Shiying decreased by 698 yuan due to floods, totaling 45,420 yuan, exceeding the total amount of increased expenditure in the third year. The remaining counties such as Huaiyin, Yangzhong, Fengxian, Gaochun, and Dongtai only increased by 1,000 to 6,000 yuan.

(8) In the first year, there were 37 counties with expenditures exceeding 10,000 yuan (Wujin 94,510 yuan, Funing 10,116 yuan). In the fifth year, there were 44 counties with expenditures exceeding 10,000 yuan (Shanghai 190,750 yuan, Shuyang 10,290 yuan). In the tenth year, there were 48 counties with expenditures exceeding 10,000 yuan (Shanghai 337,498 yuan, Jingjiang 12,155 yuan). In the fifteenth year, there were 50 counties with expenditures exceeding 10,000 yuan (Wuxi 190,985 yuan, Jingjiang 10,029 yuan). In the twentieth year, only Gaoyou (1,540 yuan) and Yangzhong (6,996 yuan) had expenditures reduced to less than 10,000 yuan due to floods.

(9) Among the expenditures of each county since the twentieth year, the lowest expenditure was 500 yuan in Yangzhong and 521 yuan in Lishui in the first year, and the highest expenditure was 362,900 yuan in Wuxian in the eighteenth year, with a difference of 725.8 times (the difference between Wujin, the county with the highest expenditure in the first year, and Zhong, is 109 times).

(10) Comparing the expenditures of each county between the twentieth year and the first year, the largest increase was 166,996 yuan in Rugao, with an increase of five times. The smallest increase was 6,350 yuan in Huaiyin, with an increase of one and a half times. The difference between the largest and smallest increases was 160,64 yuan, which is 26.29 times.

The Jue Lan She Art Exhibition Opens Today

The Jue Lan She is organized by Western-style painters Pang Xunqin, Dong Xiwen, Wang Jiyuan, Ni Yide, Zhang Xian, Zhou Duo, Duan Pingyou, Yang Qiuren, Yang Taiyang, etc., with the aim of absorbing modern world art and promoting China's inherent culture. The society is scheduled to hold its first art exhibition at the Chinese Art and Craft Society on Avenue Amédeé Péreire in the French Concession from today until the 16th of this month. More than 50 pieces of work by members and non-member painters will be exhibited. The quality of the works is unprecedented in the domestic art scene. Some lean towards neoclassicism, some are influenced by the Fauvist group, some express Eastern sentiments, and some yearn for the spirit of surrealism. Exquisite catalogs are available at the venue for distribution to the audience.

The Westerners' First Division League: Chinan Wins Over British Navy in First Match

11-0

Jiang and Chen Deserve Great Credit

In the Westerners' Football League, Chinan played their first match yesterday against the British Navy at Yiyuan. After 90 minutes of play, Chinan swept through, defeating them by eleven goals and returning in triumph.

Strength Is Worlds Apart

Chinan's army is nimble and can be called a formidable opponent. When Qiu Dongyan returns in the future, the inner defense will be even more impressive. Yesterday, the opponent was too weak, and the situation became one-sided. The midfield line's advance and retreat, offense and defense, were extremely capable. The forwards were quite sharp, but they sometimes made mistakes due to confusion. Jiang Shanqing's bold and forceful leg and Chen Zhenhe's lively and vigorous body were the most appreciated by the audience. Among the British Navy, it was difficult to find a better talent, except for the goalkeeper Davis.

Five Goals in a Row

At 3:00, referee Fult brought the ball into the stadium. With a whistle, Chinan deployed in the sun and began to attack the British army. Xiao Hei Tan passed the ball to Luo Haiguang, but it was blocked by Klaison. He quickly passed it short to Liu Zukan. Before Liu could make a few moves, Kelai chased it back. White, the enemy's center forward, dribbled the ball towards Chinan's defensive zone. Xu Yahui came out halfway, got the ball and passed it to Hong Bao, who went straight into the enemy's territory along the side. From afar, Luo Haiguang caught up and kicked it, but it bounced back from the goalpost. Xiao Hei Tan waited on the right and raised his foot to shoot, but Bairem rushed to interfere. Chen Zhenxiang found an opportunity to shoot, and the ball went into the net. In less than three minutes, Chen Zhenxiang's ball was intercepted, and Liang Shutang stole the ball back and passed it far to Haiguang. Under the watchful eyes of three enemies, Luo passed it beautifully over the enemy's defensive line. Xiao Hei Tan was as fast as a horse. Back and White could not stop him, and Davis was waiting to be tied up. Thus, Chinan scored another goal. Who would have thought that less than two minutes after the kickoff, Liu Zukan hooked a ball from the baseline and sent it to the center. Chen Zhenxiang nodded and the ball went into the goal again. From then on, Chinan was full of energy and invincible. Xu Yahui blocked two cars with one horse.

He jumped up and headed the ball to the side of Mei Hongbao. Thus, the iron cavalry of Chinan was seen again in the enemy's territory. They charged left and right, and the enemy had difficulty parrying. Chen Zhenxiang kicked the ball out of Davis's hands, and Luo Haiguang caught up and fired again, hitting the red mark. The enemy had lost four goals in a row, and their morale was greatly reduced. Almost half of the eastern part of the field was trampled by our national athletes. Liu Zukan fired a returning shot, and Xiao Hei Tan was also good at firing a head-on shot. The ball was headed out by Klaison for more than ten feet, and Luo Haiguang and Bairem kicked it at the same time. With a bang, the ball was kicked into the enemy's goal. The score was 5-1 in the first half.

A Half Dozen in One Go

After the attack, they decided the winner again. The British army was still depressed and had no counter-attacking power or defensive skills. Chen Zhenhe, with the assistance of Xu Yahui, broke through three levels and the enemy surrounded him. Tan Shi was cunning and sent the ball with his toe to the left wing. Liu Zukan swept across and the enemy's gate was lost again. Before three minutes had passed, Chen Zhenhe stole the ball from the enemy's goalkeeper and put it into the net. Not long after, Mei Hongshi took a corner kick, and Chen Zhenxiang was right on the spot to head it into the goal again from the shoulder of the enemy defender. The numbers were already shocking, but Liu Zukan and Chen Zhenhe were still not lenient and continued to score a goal. The British army then returned in dismay with a score of 0-11. The lineups of the two teams are attached below:

Chinan Team

Xie Quanhe Gu Shangdong Jiang Shanqing Liang Shutang Xu Yahui Zhuang Sihong Liu Zutan Luo Haiguang Chen Zhenhe Chen Zhenxiang Mei Hongbao

▲British Navy

Davis Bairem Klaison Bairut Quemeilin Kelai Qu Bin Schiaervo White Eruto Taushibu

It is said that Mr. Fairbanks will participate in the amateur open golf championship on Saturday and Sunday in Shanghai. As for the originally planned trip to the West, it is said to have been canceled. After this, he will likely travel around China awaiting his wife, Mary Pickford, to come to Shanghai in November, after which they will go to other countries together.

Local News

National Day Celebration Tomorrow

Citywide Flag Display Required

Banks and Money Exchanges to Close

Post Offices to Remain Open

Announcement from the Citizens' Association: The Shanghai Citizens' United Association issued an announcement yesterday regarding the National Day celebration, stating, "At this time of national crisis, while the Double Tenth Festival is the most glorious day of national celebration, the celebrations of the past should be suspended during this time of national crisis. Only commemorations should be held. It is hoped that all shops and citizens in the city will embrace the spirit of perseverance. On this day, flags must be displayed for one day to mark the occasion. All other ceremonies will be suspended. This is a special announcement."

Holiday for Banks and Money Exchanges: Tomorrow is the Double Tenth National Day. Banks and money exchanges in Shanghai will be closed for one day as usual. However, this year, due to the national crisis, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has announced that all sectors are not allowed to suspend business for celebrations. Nevertheless, the banks and money exchanges have regulations for annual holidays that cannot be changed temporarily, so they will still be closed as usual tomorrow. Foreign and Chinese banks along the Bund will also be closed as usual, but the Jianghai Customs will remain open.

Post Offices to Remain Open: On the National Day, post offices will remain open this year due to the national crisis. All branches have been notified to remain open as usual without granting holidays. However, the bureau has complied with the request of the preparatory committee for the National Products Exhibition in the city, and from tomorrow until the 23rd, all domestic mail will be stamped with "National Crisis Looms, Strive to Promote National Products" to promote the cause.

Results Temporarily Unannounced

According to the doctor, he needs a long period of rest. He is currently receiving various anti-parasitic injections. I must return to Nanjing tomorrow (i.e., today). Chengdu Chamber of Commerce Responds to Anti-War League Telegram

Earnestly Presenting the Sufferings of Sichuan Province

The General Association of the League to Abolish Internal War received a telegram from the Chengdu Chamber of Commerce yesterday, which reads: "To the General Association of the League to Abolish Internal War: We have received your letter and telegram. Since the founding of the Republic of China, Sichuan Province has been regarded by the central government as an uncivilized land, left to be occupied by military men who claim to be heroes. Wars are frequent, occurring every year. The oppression of the people, such as pre-collection of taxes, forced loans, and exorbitant taxes, is unprecedented and more severe than in other provinces. Even without any major events, the people are already unable to bear the burden. Now, Chengdu and Chongqing are mobilizing and deploying troops again. As your telegram states, it is clear that once the war breaks out, those who sacrifice their lives are the workers and farmers who are forced into military service, and those who lose their property are our law-abiding masses. However, after careful consideration of the environment and weighing the advantages and disadvantages, it is better to die with patience than to die from ineffective treatment. The ancients said, 'Stopping killing with killing' is what we pray for day and night. The General Association leads the country and advocates for the abolition of war. Regardless of whether your efforts will be effective in the future, we hope that you will rely on the people and not be used by any party. Plan concrete strategies and coordinate national salvation measures so that our compatriots can rest and recuperate when the war is over and not be subjected to various harsh policies. Then, the members of our association will lead tens of thousands of merchants in the city to follow in the footsteps of the gentlemen of the General Association. We hereby reply to your telegram for your consideration. Sincerely, Chengdu Chamber of Commerce."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter to Coal Mining Companies Requesting Lower Prices for Domestic Coal

Advising Factory Users to Support Coal Miners by Using Domestic Coal The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a notice yesterday to Zhongxing and twelve other coal mining companies and all industry associations, stating, "It has been investigated that coal used along the Yangtze River, besides joint ventures with foreign capital, which sell millions of tons annually, is mostly Japanese coal and Fushun coal. Since the September 18th Incident, people have switched to domestic coal in hopes of stopping the drain. However, the price difference between domestic coal and Japanese coal is nearly one-third. Recently, Chinese shipping companies also plan to switch to domestic coal, but they claim that the price difference is four taels per ton. If no other subsidies are provided, the increased cost will inevitably lead to bankruptcy during this shipping industry slump. It is clear that domestic coal must lower its price to win the market. Our chamber is aware that Chinese coal mines face difficulties such as a lack of vehicles, delayed transportation, heavy taxes, and immature technology, which increase production costs and prevent price reductions. However, without making efforts to overcome these difficulties, it will be difficult to develop the market. All mines should jointly find ways to lobby the authorities to facilitate transportation and reduce taxes. On the one hand, they should refer to the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce Mining Department Director's suggestion of joint production and sales and establish a joint marketing organization to avoid wasteful competition and save operating expenses. The selling price can then be gradually reduced. This is what the mines should do. On the other hand, factory users in this city should also support each other, understanding the difficulties faced by Chinese mines and the fear of national economic bankruptcy. Rather than increasing profits by using foreign coal, they should be willing to use domestic coal and reduce profits slightly, supporting the miners, which is to preserve industry. Our chamber is willing to use our limited strength and work hard to find a way to benefit both miners and users. We hope you will understand."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegrams Provincial and Municipal Chambers of Commerce to Organize Committees to Promote National Products

To Achieve the Effect of Collective Wisdom

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed provincial and municipal chambers of commerce yesterday, urging them to form national product promotion committees to maintain local national products. The telegram read: "To all provincial, municipal, and town chambers of commerce: Unfortunately, our country has suffered from both military invasion by Japanese寇 and continuous exploitation by foreign capital. Under this double pressure, the nation is in danger. To reverse this crisis, all merchants in our country must consciously rise up and promote and maintain the inherent national products of each region. To grasp the key, it is particularly important for chambers of commerce in all regions to uniformly organize national product promotion committees to achieve the effect of collective wisdom. In view of this, our chamber, after the inauguration of the second executive supervisory committee, immediately organized a national product promotion committee based on the rules of various committees and actively deliberated, hoping to contribute to national products. However, this matter is significant and cannot be accomplished by Shanghai alone. Therefore, we are issuing this telegram, hoping that you will take note, quickly organize national product promotion committees uniformly to facilitate contact. We deeply hope for your cooperation."

Salt Inspectorate Chief Zhu Inspects Zhejiang Province

Zhu Tingqi, Chief of the Salt Inspectorate and Director of the Salt Affairs Department, accompanied Finance Minister Song to Haizhou to inspect the Huaibei salt fields. He is now implementing the Minister's intention to thoroughly rectify the situation, starting with the fields and building warehouses to ensure production and storage, and prevent smuggling. This month, he inspected various fields in Zhejiang and reviewed tax collections and administrative matters. It is reported that after the anti-smuggling matters were merged into the branch office and the position of transport commissioner was concurrently held by the manager of the provincial branch, he was determined to rectify and eliminate long-standing malpractices, with significant results. The annual savings in administrative and anti-smuggling expenses have reached over 400,000 yuan. The tax revenue in the first nine months of this year has increased by more than 460,000 yuan compared to before the inspection. Since the abolition of the Wenshuo contractor in August, tax revenue has increased by tens of thousands of yuan. The tax police are neat and disciplined, which is very different from the past. Large quantities of smuggled salt, ranging from seventy or eighty dan to hundreds of dan, are often seized, which is rare. The annual tax police expenses are reduced by more than 100,000 yuan compared to the past. The management of salt along the 80-90 li coastline of Yuyao, including weighing, collecting, and releasing, is well-organized. As the largest field in Zhejiang, it is planned to start with the personnel there and further tighten the rectification to ensure maximum production and collection as a model for other fields. The policy of changing from boiling to drying salt should also be slightly modified according to local conditions. It is estimated that the annual tax revenue can be increased by several million yuan. He has instructed Feng Ruliang, the manager of the Zhejiang branch and concurrently the salt transport commissioner, to propose measures for implementation as soon as possible.

British Educator Dr. Clay Arrives in Shanghai

Dr. Clay, a famous British educator, has arrived in Shanghai with his wife to visit their daughter. They will stay for more than a month. Dr. Clay served as the headmaster of Holloway County School in North London for thirty years before retiring last winter due to old age. The London County Council has ten technical education schools, and his school is one of them. This type of technical school was first created by Hogg. Hogg was taking a walk in London one night when he saw a group of children gambling. Feeling sorry that they were wasting their valuable time, he invited them to his residence to teach them technical skills. As the results were excellent, the practice was adopted throughout the city. The ten schools in London initially planned to offer all subjects, but later found it difficult to implement, so each school specialized in several subjects. Holloway County School offered (1) a preparatory class for students seeking a science degree from the University of London, with 400 students; (2) an architecture class with about 1,400 students; (3) a rubber manufacturing class with about 300 students; and (4) a musical instrument manufacturing class with about 400 students. In addition, there was a women's class studying domestic economics and marriage problems. This excellent technical school method can be promoted in our country. It is said that the chief engineer of the Shanghai 浚浦局, Charles Lay, graduated from the architecture class of this school.

New Pacific Navigation News

Mr. Kuang Bingshun, an overseas Chinese in the United States, has recently partnered with an American business to establish the Chinese American Shipping Company. Its organization has a total of fifteen directors, of which overseas Chinese occupy twelve seats, and American businessmen only three. Mr. Kuang was elected as the general manager and established the head office in San Francisco, with branch offices in Vancouver, Seattle, and Portland. Three diesel-powered engine ships have been leased from the Danish company, East Asiatic Company, with each ship flying the Chinese flag. The first ship, Guangzhou (MS Lutlandia), arrived in Shanghai a week ago and has now set sail for Hong Kong. The second and third ships, MSS "Selandia" and MS Fufstria, will depart from the United States for Shanghai successively at the end of this year and next spring. At that time, a schedule will be arranged, once a month. It is noted that the Guangzhou is very clean and tidy because it is powered by diesel. The ship is 400 feet long, 55 feet wide, with a displacement of 10,500 tons and a deadweight of 7,600 tons. The dining room, smoking room, and conversation rooms are fully equipped. The open deck is spacious, with eleven cabins accommodating forty-five guests. The rooms are large and well-arranged, with a bathroom and toilet between every two rooms, connected by interior doors for easy access, which is very convenient. Both Chinese and Western meals are available on board, allowing guests to choose as they please. There are Chinese waiters providing attentive service. The first-class fare from Shanghai to the United States is US$120, and from Shanghai to Hong Kong, it only costs 60 Chinese yuan. It is heard that this time the ship came to China with the support of overseas Chinese, and the fare is fair, so there are many passengers. The Shanghai and Hong Kong affairs are still managed by the East Asiatic Company. China Travel Service on Sichuan Road also sells all passenger tickets.
