Navy Adjutant Zeng Guoxi Suicide

Returned from Japan, the Reason Unknown

Zeng Guoxi, a Fujianese naval torpedo camp adjutant, was sent to Japan to study torpedoes. He had just graduated and ranked first. He was ordered to return to China by the Ministry a few days ago. After arriving in Shanghai, he stayed for only one day before going to Beijing to report. He was assigned by the Navy Department to the Chuqian warship as a torpedo officer. Unexpectedly, Mr. Zeng, for some unknown reason, suddenly committed suicide with a pistol in the Beijing camp the night before, and died immediately. Later, the Navy Department telegraphed Shanghai to inform his brother, Zeng Guosheng (currently serving as a new ship supervisor). Mr. Zeng was extremely saddened after receiving the news. Minister Chen of the Ministry was also quite saddened after hearing the news and will provide condolences in accordance with regulations. Zeng was 28 years old and worked very hard. His family life was also very fulfilling, so the reason for this suicide is difficult for outsiders to guess. According to reports, Chen Minghui, captain of the Navy Rensheng ship, also committed suicide a month ago due to economic difficulties, so Zeng's death is the second suicide case in the Navy.

Record of Conflicts Between Hukuai and Merchants in Shanghai Rice Shops

Merchants Put Forward Conditions and Stop Shipping

Rice Industry Asks Party and Government to Stop It

The Shanghai rice shipping merchants, previously suffering invisible losses due to the use of heavy pecks by the Hukuai in various rice shops, organized a petition to request assistance. The Social Affairs Bureau issued a public notice. Since the arrest of the Hukuai on the 5th, all rice shops uniformly stopped pecking rice on the 6th. After mediation, pecking resumed yesterday morning. Unfortunately, a conflict occurred, and many people were injured. The details are as follows:

Public Notice by the Social Affairs Bureau: The Social Affairs Bureau issued a public notice stating that the Lianyi Association of rice shipping merchants in the South City reported that since the Hukuai fee was abolished by the Association's resolution, the Hukuai used heavy pecks, causing considerable losses, and requested relief. The petition was submitted. The Hukuai are workers employed by the rice shops and should act as intermediaries, representing the rice shops to seek fairness for both buyers and sellers. How can they use their skills to implement heavy pecks and collect illegal fees? Moreover, heavy and light pecks have been prohibited by the Bureau's public notice. Now that the Hukuai are using heavy pecks because the rice shipping merchants have abolished the Hukuai fee, it is illegal if true and should be strictly prohibited. In the future, if Hukuai are found to be using heavy or light pecks, or soliciting Hukuai fees,

rice shipping merchants or rice shops are allowed to report to the Bureau. Once verified, they will be severely punished without leniency. Based on the aforementioned situation, a public notice is hereby issued for general knowledge. This notice.

Hukuai Not Opening Pecks: On the 5th of this month, the Social Affairs Bureau received a report from rice shipping merchants that the Hukuai in various rice shops were still using heavy pecks. The Bureau dispatched Mao Shenghe, an official from the Fourth Section, to stop them. Together with the rice shipping merchants, they arrested Yao Heshang, a Hukuai from Hengxingxie Rice Shop, and Zhang Amao, a Hukuai from Juxingsheng Rice Shop, and detained them in the First Precinct, First Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau. All the Hukuai were angered and went on strike, causing the rice shops to stop pecking rice. Fortunately, after the police station inquired, they were released. The Social Affairs Bureau, considering that the suspension of rice pecking had a significant impact on the people's food supply, immediately instructed the Public Security Bureau to resume rice pecking immediately and try to persuade them. It was not until yesterday morning that a solution was reached, and the Hukuai resumed work, and the rice shops resumed pecking rice.

The Cause of the Conflict: Yesterday morning, the Hukuai from various rice shops went to work at the soy and rice industry pier on the Bund. At 10:00 AM, the Shanghai South Rice Shipping Merchants Lianyi Association rushed to the scene, opposing heavy pecks and stopping them. At that time, a conflict occurred between the merchants and the Hukuai. The pier police tried to persuade them, initially interfering with other people's businesses, but were eventually confronted by the merchants, and the police uniform was torn. Policeman Su Shenren was injured. Fortunately, Yi Zuanren, the director of the First Precinct, First Sub-bureau of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, rushed to the scene with police to suppress the situation. Merchants Ren Jinquan, Zou Asong, Zhou Longgui, Shen Jinsheng, and Mu Asong were also injured to varying degrees. The director of the sub-bureau detained the injured merchants Shen Jinsheng and Mu Asong in the police station. The rest of the injured were sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injuries were minor, and they were discharged soon after.

Petition from Merchants: The Shanghai West Rice Shipping Merchants Lianyi Society gathered more than a hundred merchants yesterday morning and organized the "Shanghai South Rice Shipping Petition Group." They submitted a petition to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau requesting: (1) punish Zhu Zixiang and Yan Xiaoquan, rice industry leaders, for instigating the strike to coerce; (2) investigate and punish A Mei, a Hukuai from Wanxing Rice Shop, for instructing Hukuai to use heavy pecks; (3) compensate for losses during the Hukuai strike; (4) re-arrest the Hukuai Zhang Amao and Yao Heshang and severely punish them; (5) deny the qualifications of Hukuai and request that merchants conduct their own pecking; (6) establish fair pecks and eliminate malpractices. Zhou Minggang from the Fourth Section received them and promised to forward the petition to the director for handling.

Rice Merchants Went on Strike Yesterday: Yesterday morning, after the conflict between the Hukuai and rice shipping merchants and the injury of Ren Jinquan and others, all the merchants were very indignant. In addition to continuing to petition the Social Affairs Bureau, they also announced a strike at 10:00 AM.

Meetings of Two Guilds: The Soy and Rice Industry Guild and the Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cakes Guild convened a joint meeting of colleagues from the soy, rice, miscellaneous grains, and oil cakes industries yesterday afternoon on the third floor of the Miscellaneous Grains Guild. Zhu Zixiang reported that the Rice Shipping Lianyi Association was interfering with rice pecking, dragging away Hukuai, and behaving abnormally, resulting in a market closure. After the Social Affairs Bureau advised them to reopen the market, the shops complied with the order and resumed pecking this morning. Unexpectedly, the boat owners gathered sixty or seventy people, rushed to the pier, and prevented rice pecking, even beating and injuring the police officers and tearing their clothes and hats, causing the Hukuai to be afraid to board the ships and peck rice. Nine people who committed the violence have been arrested. This matter harms the interests of the industry. Please quickly devise a solution. After discussion among the merchants, Gu Xinyi, Cai Yukun, Chen Ziyi, Yan Xiaoquan, Zhu Zixiang, and Fu Qiangeng were nominated to go to the Municipal Party Department, Social Affairs Bureau, and Public Security Bureau to present the situation of the boat owners' harassment and request a stop to it. At the same time, a document was submitted to the Ministry of Industry and the Municipal Government for review and handling.

Post-Incident Prevention: After receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau, fearing that the dispute would escalate, dispatched additional police teams to the soy and rice market pier to station there. At the same time, they also advised the Hukuai in various rice shops to work as usual. Therefore, at about 1:00 PM, the Hukuai in various rice shops resumed work as usual. In the evening, the police teams were withdrawn, and four armed police officers were dispatched by the First Precinct Police Station to guard the area for prevention.

Silk Factories in Hongkou District to Resume Work This Morning on a Trial Basis

If Workers Do Not Return to Work, They Prepare to Close Down

Government Sent Personnel Yesterday to Advise the Union

The labor dispute in the city's silk factories is worsening after the Social Affairs Bureau's mediation broke down. The factories in the Hongkou district are scheduled to sound the whistle this morning to resume work, but it is still uncertain whether the striking female workers will return to work.

Yuyuan and Other Resumption of Work: After the female workers of Yuyuan Silk Factory on Guoging Road and Chuxin Silk Factory on Manchuria Road went on strike again, the factory accepted the advice of the Silk Factory Industry Association and sounded the whistle at 5:30 AM yesterday morning, announcing the resumption of work. At the same time, they were protected by the Fourth District Water Police of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. At that time, although the female workers' conditions had not yet been specifically addressed, they entered the factory and resumed work for the sake of their livelihood. By about 6:00 AM, the female workers of the two factories had completely entered the factory and resumed work. The workers in the Zhabei district and the concession area also worked as usual, and fortunately, no incidents occurred.

Hongkou District to Resume Work Today: In the Hongkou district, the Xiangcheng and other silk factories, excluding Yichang, which has been closed, total eleven. Since the strike on the 23rd of last month, it has been more than ten days. After repeated mediation by the government, no solution has been found. According to the resolution of the Second Member Congress of the Silk Factory Industry Association, it was decided to uniformly sound the whistle at 5:30 AM this morning to announce the resumption of work. At the same time, the Fifth District, Fourth Sub-bureau of the Municipal Public Security Bureau was requested to send additional police officers for protection. The factory supervisors informed the female workers in advance that if the workers did not return to work after the resumption of work, they would prepare to close down and move elsewhere to do business. However, it is still uncertain whether the female workers will return to work.

Government Sent Personnel to Advise: The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly conducted mediation with the Municipal Party Department regarding the silk factory industry's strike dispute. However, because the employer representatives refused the conditions put forward by the union and insisted on the labor-management contract method of July 8, mediation could not proceed. In addition to submitting the handling process to the director for instructions, in order to avoid the expansion of the strike, the Bureau specially sent staff yesterday to advise the Fourth District Silk Reeling Industry Union, etc.

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Officially Discloses the Shanghai Workers' Cost of Living Index

The book "Shanghai Workers' Cost of Living Index" compiled by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau took three years from planning to completion. More than 40 people conducted on-site surveys. It was originally scheduled to be published on January 30 this year, but the manuscripts were destroyed in the Commercial Press fire. After reprinting and correcting, it was finally completed. At the same time, the materials for the 20th year were added, and it was published by Zhonghua Book Company. The book is based on a household livelihood survey of 305 worker families, weighted by consumption, and includes retail prices of 60 items, divided into five categories, from January 15th to December 20th. Issues related to the investigation and compilation, such as weighted averages, price surveys, calculation formulas, and price base periods, are discussed in detail. The trends of classified and total indices over the years are analyzed in order, and the reasons for the rise and fall are explained in detail. In addition to the indices and prices over the years, important domestic cost of living indices and retail prices are also attached for reference. The system of weights and measures has been changed to the newly promulgated and municipal system. Mr. Cai Yuanpei of the Academia Sinica said, "It will undoubtedly benefit the study of Shanghai labor affairs and the Chinese labor movement." Mr. An Lide, Commercial Counselor of the United States, said, "It will be of great contribution to those who want to clearly understand the actual situation of China's industrialization." Professor Fang Xianting of Nankai University said, "The cost of living index compiled by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is the most extensive in scope." He also said, "It is enough to prove that Chinese people are gradually paying attention to the use of indices." "It can also make the complicated and unstable situation in the current economic order more clear."

Municipal Government Issues Guidelines for Trade Union Elections

Standards for Generating Representatives Specified

The municipal government, in accordance with the guidelines for trade union congress elections sent by the Ministry of Industry and already promulgated, stipulates in Article 1 that if the number of trade union members is too large to convene a general membership meeting, a representative congress may be convened in accordance with Article 13 of the Trade Union Law. Article 2 stipulates that the representatives of the representative congress shall be directly elected by all members in accordance with the following table: 100 to 500 members shall be divided into five groups, and for every 500 members added thereafter, five groups shall be added, with each group electing one representative. Article 3 stipulates that if the remaining number of people after grouping is more than half of the proportion in the previous table, another group may be divided; if it is less than half, it shall be included in the last group for combined election. Article 4 stipulates that only those who have a trade union membership certificate are eligible to be representative electors and candidates. Article 5 stipulates that representative elections shall be conducted by registered voting. Article 6 stipulates that a trade union director shall preside over the representative election, and the trade union supervisor shall be the election supervisor. Article 7 stipulates that members who cannot fill out the ballot may ask the election supervisor to fill it out on their behalf, but they must sign or seal it themselves. Article 8 stipulates that after the representatives are elected, the chairman and the election supervisor shall prepare a certificate in accordance with the law and hand it over to the elected representatives and report it to the trade union director. Article 9 stipulates that the form of the representative certificate shall be as follows: "Representative Certificate of the Trade Union Congress of [Name of Trade Union], hereby elects [Name of Representative] as the attending representative, [Name of Chairman], [Name of Election Supervisor], certifies." Article 10 stipulates that representatives attending the trade union congress shall present the election attendance certificate and their own membership certificate to the qualification review committee of the congress upon reporting to the congress. If their certificate or membership certificate is inconsistent, they shall be submitted to the congress to cancel their representative qualification. Article 11 stipulates that the representative election rules of the congress shall be formulated by each trade union in accordance with these guidelines and submitted to the competent authorities for approval and implementation. These guidelines shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Social Affairs Bureau Drafts Measures for Fire Insurance Compensation in Disaster Areas

Municipal Government Approves Claims Committee

The Shanghai Disaster Area Fire Insurance Claims Committee previously requested the municipal government to quickly find a way to provide substantial assistance and submitted a report to the municipal government. Yesterday, the municipal government specifically

issued a directive stating: The submission has been noted. This case was previously reported to the government by the Disaster Area Fire Insurance Compensation Association, requesting assistance. The Social Affairs Bureau was ordered to review the case and submit three proposed handling methods: (1) From a rational and emotional point of view, this compensation cannot be fully paid according to the amount, nor can it be completely unpaid. The Fire Insurance Compensation Research Association should be responsible for quickly clarifying and studying the disaster situation of the insured households in various places to determine whether or not to pay compensation; (2) After any insured household is determined to have no compensation, the insurance company should refund the premium that has been paid; (3) Adopt the proposal of the Lawyers Association and Accountants Association to issue public bonds as a means of relief. The reason for increasing the premium and using the public bond fund for the insured is still taken from the insured, and the insurance industry is not fundamentally affected. However, foreign merchants operating should also be required to bear corresponding obligations. The three proposed points were deemed to be fair, and the bureau was ordered to convene representatives of Chinese and foreign insurance associations in this city and all relevant parties to properly formulate specific measures and submit them for approval. The aforementioned situation is now in accordance with the previous order, except that the Social Affairs Bureau is ordered to comply with the previous order and quickly handle the case and report it.

Municipal Health Bureau Plans to Establish a Yangjing Model Health District

The Wusong Model Health District Is Temporarily Suspended

The city originally had two model health districts, Wusong and Gaoqiao. The Wusong Model District was jointly operated by the Municipal Health Bureau and the Medical College of the Central University. The Gaoqiao Model District was solely managed by the Municipal Health Bureau. The funding was previously subsidized by the American oil tycoon Rockefeller. Recently, the American oil tycoon stopped the subsidies, and the Wusong Model

District was almost completely destroyed by the Shanghai War and could not be restored. The Municipal Health Bureau changed its policy, temporarily suspending the Wusong Model District, while the Gaoqiao Model District was jointly operated with the Medical College of the Central University. A new model district is being planned and built in Yangjing. It is reported that the plan has been approved by the Municipal Government. In terms of funding, the planned construction cost is 13,000 yuan, the equipment cost is 3,500 yuan (including soil filling, ditching, pipe lighting, wires, and other sanitary equipment), and the start-up cost is 2,500 yuan (including instruments, medical equipment, medicines, printed materials, stationery, miscellaneous expenses, etc.), totaling 19,000 yuan. In addition to the 6,000 yuan raised by Pan Weibing, the former Yangjing District Municipal Committee member, the rest will be allocated by the Municipal Government and has been completely resolved. Therefore, the Bureau is actively proceeding with the construction of the new model district and will be able to open it around March next year.

Hu Xiyuan's Letter to the National Private Electric Power Association

Since its establishment, the National Private Electric Power Association has been well-organized, well-managed, and has achieved remarkable results. However, the association has foreign merchant members, and the association's charter and application form are all in English, which causes outsiders to misunderstand the truth. Now, Hu Xituyuan of the Electric Power Industry has written a letter to the association as follows: Dear Sirs (omitted above), I recently heard of your association's charter and the solicitation of membership, combining the power of the country to seek the development of the electric power industry. The purpose is just and great, and I admire it very much. Although I am not talented, I have been in the electric power industry for a long time. I would like to discuss with my colleagues what I have seen and heard: (1) The name and reality should be consistent. Since your association is named the National Private Electric Power Association, then in terms of territory, it is naturally limited to the territory under the jurisdiction of the Republic of China. In terms of people, it should also be the industry operated by the people of the Republic of China. Now, Article 3 of the charter stipulates that the qualifications of members include a supporting member item, and

foreign electrical appliance companies can also be included, and stipulate the membership fee that should be paid each month. I think it is not possible. For the sake of exchanging knowledge and promoting culture, the development of the European and American electric power industries is more than several times greater than that of our country. How can they condescend to the scope and be willing to be a member and bear the annual expenses? How can we ask the guides who import culture to join the association and collect their membership fees? Even if there are foreign merchants who are willing to come and are happy to transport, their intentions are different. This is the first point that should be discussed in fact. If it is said that this association is not enough to be called a union without borrowing from other mountains, then it is already named the National Private

Electric Power Association, and the national private electric power industry is naturally the main body. Why add supporting members among the members? Why add foreign companies in addition to domestic companies? This is even more suspicious and should be discussed in two (2) The charter and application form should be changed to Chinese. The text is the expression of a country's culture. All independent countries respect their national text. Our country has suffered from the invasion of great powers for a long time, either by military force, or by economy, or by culture, and their invasion purposes are all the same. In recent years, the Chinese people have become quite aware, so the foreign language documents used in the future are gradually changed to Chinese, and the intention is very good. Your association is a large group with a nationally recognized organization, and the charter and application form sent are all in English. Outsiders are unpredictable, thinking that this is a group of international organizations. But who knows that it is a union of our national private electric power industry. Although the matter is trivial, it is very important to the public opinion, and this should be discussed even more. The above two points are said from the beginning. I am not talented, and I venture to present my words, and I hope to be taught (omitted below).

Increase in Japanese Goods Imported to China in September

Mainly Silk and Cotton Textiles

The Japanese Commercial Counselor's Office in Shanghai received a telegram from Tokyo yesterday stating that Japan's exported goods in September were worth a total of 140 million Japanese yen. In that month, due to the increase in raw silk, cotton woven piece goods, cotton yarn, silk woven piece goods, and rayon to Europe, the United States, and China, the trade surplus reached 44 million Japanese yen, an increase of 38 million Japanese yen over the same month last year. From January to September this year, the total trade deficit reached 115 million Japanese yen, an increase of 39 million Japanese yen compared to the same period last year. In August, Japanese goods imported to China were worth a total of 17 million Japanese yen, with a trade surplus of 12 million Japanese yen. From January to August this year, the total trade surplus with China reached 54 million Japanese yen, a decrease of 14 million Japanese yen compared to the same period last year. Furthermore, dividing and analyzing by region, imports to Central China increased by 3% compared to the same period last year, imports to North China increased by 1.3%, and imports to South China decreased significantly, decreasing by 73%. Goods shipped from China to Japan increased by 0.8% in North China and 47% in South China, while decreasing by 30% in Central China. Goods imported to the Three Eastern Provinces in August were worth a total of 12 million Japanese yen, with a trade surplus of 8 million Japanese yen, an increase of 95% over the same month last year.

Local News

The Case of the Robbery and Assassination of Wu Guangzhong at the Changxing Coal Mine

Zhou Mingshan Also Implicated

Identified by Maid Qiuhong

All Suspects Temporarily Not Transferred

A Seven-Day Extension for Investigation

Li Yangyuan, the Detective Chief of the Second Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Government Security Team, investigated that the Changxing Coal Mine Bureau in Changxing County, Zhejiang Province, was raided by a large gang of bandits armed with weapons in November of last year. The bandits robbed over five thousand yuan, opened fire to resist arrest, killed Police Chief Lu, and seized over ten firearms. It was discovered that some of the bandits had fled to Shanghai, so he led detectives Yao Bailin, Zhou Mingshan, etc., to Shanghai. They requested the Old Zha police station to send more Chinese and foreign detectives to Room 89 of the Juelu Hotel on Xizang Road and Room 28 of the Xindahua Hotel on Fuzhou Road. They arrested four suspects: Song Jiande, Wu Jigui, Zhang Shaoliang, and Yao Jieshen. Two box-type pistols and fifty-nine rounds of ammunition were found in Room 28. After examination, it was found that the firearms were all stamped with the seal of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau. They were handed over to the First Special District Court, which ordered them to be detained for investigation and interrogation. This matter has been reported in this newspaper.

Assassination of Wu Guangzong The police station has now found that Wu Guangzong, the director of the Hydrographic Survey Bureau, was assassinated on the 21st of last month at 8 a.m. While he was sleeping in his residence at No. 16 Ningli, Fangxie Road in the city, several thugs broke into his house, forced their way upstairs, and shot him, causing his death. It has been confirmed that Song Jiande, Zhang Shaoliang, and Zhou Mingshan (also known as Zhou Asi), a detective of the Second Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Team, colluded to commit the murder.

Robbery on Wuzhou Road At 6 p.m. on the 24th of last month, the home of Chen Rongsheng, a resident of No. 1040 Wuzhou Road, was raided by four armed robbers who stole valuables worth 140 yuan. It has also been confirmed that Zhou Mingshan, along with Song and Zhang, and other accomplices who are still at large, committed the robbery. The firearms stamped with the seal of the Municipal Police Bureau were lost by the Zhabei Fourth District Police Department during the Sino-Japanese War. Therefore, the Chinese and foreign detectives detained Zhou Mingshan.

Identifying the Real Culprits Wu Guangzong's wife, Zhong Huizhen, his family maid, Qiuhong, and Chen Rongsheng's son, Chen Akang, were summoned to the police station separately. Zhou Mingshan was made to change his clothes and mixed among the group of suspects for each person to identify. Qiuhong immediately identified Zhou as one of the murderers. Yesterday morning, Zhou, along with Song, Wu, Zhang, and Yao, were all sent to the First Special District Court. Judge Feng Shide conducted the interrogation, and Chief Prosecutor Wang also attended the court to perform his duties.

All Temporarily Not Transferred After arriving in court, the representative of the Municipal Police Bureau and the Zhejiang Provincial Detective Chief Li Yangyuan each stated their reasons, competing to request the transfer of the suspects. However, Detective Li still defended his colleague Zhou Mingshan. The police station lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated the findings of the investigation, arguing that since the defendants had committed robbery within the concession, the transfer should be delayed until the robbery case was thoroughly investigated and concluded before further action was taken.

Witness Testimony Next, Chen Akang testified that three robbers came that day, all carrying handguns. He only recognized Song Jiande and Zhang Shaoliang. Chen Rongsheng's wife testified that Yao Jieshen had previously rented a room upstairs in her house, and Song, Wu, and Zhang all came to visit Yao every day. However, she was out when the robbery occurred, so she did not witness it. Wu's maid, Qiuhong, testified that four people came that morning. They first talked to the homeowner's bodyguard, Lao Xu, for half an hour, so she clearly recognized the faces of all four people. Besides Zhou Mingshan, the others were Song, Wu, and Zhang.

Defendant Testimony When questioned, Song Jiande and Zhang Shaoliang both stated that Zhou Mingshan had given them the handguns, and they returned them to Zhou after the robbery, who then distributed the stolen money, three yuan and five yuan respectively. Yao Jieshen claimed that Zhou Mingshan provided the money to rent the room at the Xindahua Hotel, and he claimed he did not know who hid the firearms in the room. Zhou Mingshan completely denied the robbery and the murder of Director Wu, claiming that he came to Shanghai to arrest bandits and was being falsely accused by them. He requested a detailed investigation. The judge then ordered the defendants to be returned to custody and extended the period for seven days to investigate and continue the interrogation.

One Bandit in Lu Shaotang Kidnapping Case Sent Back for Retrial

Kidnapping Crime Already Received Clemency

Gun Murder of Bodyguard Requires Further Investigation

Lu Shaotang, a compradore at the Fairchild & Co., was kidnapped at dusk on December 18th two years ago when his car passed the intersection of Nanjing Road and Yunnan Road by Fei Shuaisong and others. The Russian bodyguard hired by Lu, Mao Taisituluo, who was sitting in the car, was shot and killed by the bandits. Afterward, the police rescued Lu and successively captured many of the bandits, all of whom were convicted by the First Special District Court. Those sentenced to death, except for Li Changyuan from Tianjin, are still imprisoned awaiting execution. The others, such as Fei Shuaisong, have already been executed. Li's death sentence had also been approved by the Jiangsu Provincial Government, but at that time the National Government was issuing a general amnesty, so Li's execution was temporarily suspended. After re-examination by the Jiangsu Provincial Government, a doubt was discovered. According to the amnesty regulations, kidnapping offenders could receive clemency, but those who committed premeditated murder were not included in the amnesty. Li Changyuan's kidnapping of Lu Shaotang with his accomplices was confirmed, but whether Li was also involved in the shooting of Lu's bodyguard required further investigation. Therefore, the Second Branch of the High Court ordered Shen Jiayi, the president of the court, to instruct Zhou Xianjue, the president of the First Special District Court, to re-examine the murder portion of the case to ensure caution. After the Special Court notified the police station, yesterday morning, detectives were dispatched to the Western Prison to bring Li Changyuan to court, and the accomplice Hu Mingde and witnesses were also summoned separately. Judge Feng interrogated them. Li Changyuan mistakenly believed that the reason for the retrial was to absolve him of his guilt, so he denied all the circumstances of the kidnapping that were interrogated in court, and even denied what he had previously confessed. Hu Mingde and Lu Shaotang's two drivers could not definitively prove whether Li Changyuan was present when the shooting occurred. However, police station lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated that, according to the confessions of other accomplices in the case, Li delivered the handgun to the hotel, and Li and his accomplices were in the same car when the shooting occurred, so Li was not only present at the scene, but had conspired beforehand and should not be entitled to the amnesty. The court also appointed a lawyer to defend Li, and after being instructed by Chief Prosecutor Wang, Judge Feng scheduled the sentencing for the morning of the 15th of this month, and the defendant was returned to custody.

Robbery and Killing on Yu Tong Road: One Bandit Captured, One Killed

Police Bravery in Apprehending Robbers Commendable

At 9:55 p.m. the night before last, when Wu Jinshan's Wu Yilong noodle shop at No. 89 Yu Tong Road, Zhabei, was about to close, four robbers suddenly appeared. Two were wearing black cloth short shirts and trousers, and two were wearing blue cloth short shirts and trousers. They were bald and spoke with a Jiangbei accent. They carried three handguns, and one unarmed robber stood guard at the door. One robber walked into the shop, and two robbers went upstairs, driving Wu's family to the roof, prohibiting them from making any noise. Under Wu's bed, they searched and stole 140 yuan in banknotes. Then they went downstairs and searched the shop assistant, Zhong Chengcai, taking three yuan in silver, four yuan in banknotes, and ten jiao in small silver coins. Wu's relative, Cang Fa, happened to be visiting and staying overnight in the shop, so he was also robbed of 15.40 yuan. When the three robbers saw that they had achieved their goal, they immediately ran out. Before leaving, they turned back and took a felt hat from the counter. Wu Jinshan immediately chased after them, shouting for help. Police officers at posts No. 15 and No. 3 nearby heard the alarm and urgently reported to the Second Sub-bureau of the Fourth District. Section Chief Hou Zhai immediately dispatched Inspector Lin to lead a large number of police officers to surround and capture the robbers in three directions: Yu Tong Road, Guangfu Road, and Guangzhao Road. Seeing that they were being closely pursued, the robbers split up and fled west. In a moment of desperation, one robber fled into a thatched house on Chang'an Road. Seeing that police officer Shao Xueyi was closely pursuing him, he turned back and opened fire to resist arrest. Shao returned fire, and both sides exchanged four or five shots. The robber was shot and killed by Shao. At the same time, Inspector Lin also captured a robber near Guangfu Road. The other two robbers escaped due to the darkness. The captured robber was taken to the Second Sub-bureau, where, after interrogation, he confessed his name as Liu Jinbiao, 25 years old, from Funing. The dead robber was named Zhang Ziyu, who had previously visited friends unsuccessfully and earned a living by pulling a rickshaw. On the first day of this month, he met Cao Xiaosizi, who was on the run, at Xinqiao in the Sampan Factory. Cao gave him two small silver coins because he saw that he was poor, and asked him to go to his thatched house on the night before last (the 7th) to discuss matters. He kept his promise and went. Cao Xiaosizi told him to stand guard at the door of the Wu Yilong noodle shop. After Cao Xiaosizi finished robbing the shop, he gave him 24 yuan in silver and a felt hat. After verifying his confession, the sub-bureau found 24 yuan in silver and a felt hat on his person. Section Chief Hou then strictly ordered all police officers to pursue the two robbers who were still at large and bring them to justice. The body of the dead robber was reported to the court for inspection by the local bailiff. The sub-bureau has prepared a document to report Liu Jinbiao to the General Bureau for further investigation.

The 12th Anniversary Exhibition and Amusement Fair of the China National Road Construction Association opened at the New World at noon yesterday. The inside and outside of the venue were newly decorated and extremely beautiful. At the entrance was a plaque inscribed by the Executive Yuan with the words "Roads as a Means to Prosperity". Inside the venue, there were many oil paintings showing the road conditions of various provinces and cities, as well as hundreds of maps showing the trunk lines and systems of roads in various provinces, analyzed in great detail. Inside the small park east of the Peking Opera theater, a special exhibition room was set up to display various models, which were particularly elaborate. These included a model of the construction of the Zhengzheng Road sewer in Wuhan, a model of the highway in Beijing (the entire road from Xichang'anmen to Xichang'anjie), a model of Zhongshan Park in Wuhan, a model of the construction of the Yanjiekou Road in Wuhan, a model of the Shahe Bei Da Mu Bridge in Hebei Province (the bridge is thirty-eight zhang long and one zhang six chi wide), and a model of the street route in the urban area of Wuhan, totaling dozens of types. There were also hundreds of photographs. On the left side of the Peking Opera theater hung a calligraphy by Wu Tiecheng: "If 400 million compatriots smoke a few fewer cigarettes and drink a few fewer glasses of yellow wine every day, they can complete millions of miles of automobile roads." On the right side was a calligraphy by Wang Zhengting: "If I don't work hard to promote road construction to save the country, I will be sorry to the people, and I will be sorry to the country. If people don't join the association and promote road construction to save the country, people are sorry to me, and people are sorry to the country. Everyone should try their best to show the spirit of construction." In terms of entertainment, in addition to the various high-class entertainments originally at the New World, all the male and female stars of the Star Company performed Peking Opera and the latest drama "The Test of Love" on stage. Yesterday, more than a thousand people came, and the traffic was bustling, creating a great sensation. In addition, all the entertainments at the Amusement Fair of the association were carefully selected. The most rare thing was the performance of famous male and female stars at sea. After the stars of the Star Company performed for three days, the performances of the stars of the Tianyi Company will begin on the 11th. The program for the first day (i.e. the 11th) includes Yuan Meiyun and Yuan Hanyun's "Fishing and Killing Family", Li Minghui's solo singing, and Hu Shanshan, Zhang Zhenduo, etc.'s "The Clock". The program for the second day (i.e. the 12th) includes Hu Shanshan, Xiao Zhengzhong, and Shu Lijuan's "Selling Oneself for Burial", Yuan Meiyun and Yuan Hanyun's "June Snow", and Xuan Jinglin, Zhang Zhenduo, etc.'s "The Clock". The program for the third day (i.e. the 13th) includes Dai Nanfang's (Kun Opera) "Thinking of the Secular World", Yuan Meiyun and Yuan Hanyun's "Fenhe Bay", and Xuan Jinglin, Zhang Zhenduo, etc.'s "The Clock", etc. masterpieces.

Centenarian Mother Celebrates Her Birthday Today

There is a rural woman named Gu Yao on the Caojiaqiao in west Shanghai, between Jiaozhou Road and Yuyuan Road. She is already one hundred years old, and today is her birthday. Her children and grandchildren are holding a celebration for her. Gu Yao's family is quite wealthy and owns a lot of farmland. Her husband passed away 25 years ago, and he was the same age as her. He was 75 years old when he passed away. Gu Yao's family used to be engaged in farming. After the opening of Shanghai as a concession, the land in western Shanghai became valuable, so Gu Yao became even wealthier. However, she is still able to manage her household frugally and work hard as before. She has three sons and two daughters, three grandsons and five granddaughters, three great-grandsons, and four great-granddaughters. She also has many nephews, nieces and great-nieces. However, her eldest son has already passed away. When her husband passed away, Gu Yao divided her family property into three shares. The eldest son's family still lives in the old house in Caojiaqiao, while the second and youngest sons have built new residences on Yuyuan Road. Today's celebration is being held in the new house of her youngest son, Gu Jiatang, on Yuyuan Road. However, Gu Yao does not like living in Western-style houses and still lives in her old house in Caojiaqiao. Gu Yao is very frugal in her life, and her diet and clothing are regular, so she is still quite healthy. She says that she has never had any illnesses in her life, and even a slight headache is considered a major illness. She is now a hundred years old, but her movements are no different from those of a woman in her fifties. Her teeth have fallen out, her eyes are slightly blurred, and her ears are slightly deaf, which is similar to ordinary old women. She gets up at 7 a.m. every day and rests at 8 p.m. She eats one bowl of rice for each of her three meals a day and can still work as before. Three years ago, she could wash her own clothes without help, but now she still sews her own clothes if they are slightly torn. Gu Yao often admonishes her children to manage their households without extravagance. She has visited places such as the Sincere Company and traveled by car, but later said that cars are not as comfortable as rented cars, and rented cars are not as smooth as sedan chairs. She can talk about historical events vividly and is concerned about the recent changes. In modern times, people indulge in licentiousness, and it is rare to live to be a hundred years old, so today's banquet will definitely be a grand occasion.

Detailed Report of the Inauguration Ceremony of the New Clubhouse of the Young Women's Christian Association

Mayor Wu Zhongcheng Attends and Delivers Instructions

At 4 p.m. the day before yesterday, the National Association of the Chinese Christian Young Women's Christian Association held the inauguration ceremony of its new clubhouse at No. 19 Yuanmingyuan Road. More than 200 guests from all walks of life, both Chinese and foreign, attended. Mrs. Zheng Zhangcheng, president of the association, Ms. Ding Shuxian, general secretary, and all the committee members and staff cordially welcomed them. After the ceremony began at 4 p.m., Mrs. Zheng Zhangcheng first described the overview, history, and construction of the new clubhouse, generally stating that the Young Women's Christian Association has a history of more than 20 years. In the past, it has continuously worked hard on the women's movement and family and child problems. Since the September 18th Incident, it has especially devoted itself to national affairs. Now that the clubhouse has been completed, the foundation is solid. On the one hand, she thanked people from all walks of life for their encouragement and guidance over the years, and on the other hand, she hoped that they would continue to provide help. Next, Mayor Wu spoke. Mayor Wu was in high spirits that day and gave great encouragement to the achievements of the Young Women's Christian Association, generally saying that in order to build a new China, the people must rise up and take responsibility for their own affairs and work hard. The Young Women's Christian Association leads women to do their best to improve families and children, and bears a heavy responsibility, expressing infinite hope. Then, Ms. Zeng Youzong gave a speech. Ms. Zeng spoke eloquently and passionately, making profound criticisms and passionate hopes for the modern women's liberation movement, which won a round of applause. Finally, Mrs. Pan Guangjiong played a piano solo with a melodious sound, which was truly skillful. By the time the meeting ended, the city was lit up with thousands of lights, near dusk. The committee members and staff of the association still warmly guided the guests to visit the association's memorial hall, library, and office, and gave each person a copy of the association's publications as a souvenir. The new clubhouse is eight stories high, magnificent, and full of Eastern aesthetic colors. The construction cost a total of 350,000 taels, and it is related to the structure of the famous architect Mr. Li Jinpei.

Stolen Car by British Sailors Located

The Shanghai Mercury reported that the sailors who stole a Morris Cowley car in the Bund on Thursday afternoon have been identified. The sailors claimed that a Westerner had invited them to take a ride around the Bund, but they could not explain why they drove to Zhabei, injured several people, and abandoned the car. According to reports, the car was stolen by seven sailors at 2:30 p.m. on Thursday and driven into the French Concession. At that time, the police were searching everywhere, but its whereabouts were unknown. It was not until three hours later that a New Gate patrolman saw it driving across the Suzhou River. After that, it is unknown how it ended up causing trouble in Zhabei. The two headlights and two mudguards were damaged, and two Chinese people were injured. The Chinese police investigated and informed the car owner to retrieve it.

Fortune Together Steamer Grounded

French Warship Arrives for Rescue

The Fortune Together steamer, which operates on the Sichuan River, flies the French flag and is represented by Tiensin & Co. in Shanghai. The ship left Shanghai on September 29th, carrying cargo and passengers for Chongqing. On the 5th of this month, it passed Hankou. At 8 p.m. that day, the ship ran aground about 200 li upstream from Hankou. The ship was damaged and ran aground in shallow water. The shipowner was unable to get it out of the shallows, so he sent out a distress signal for help. The French warship in the Yangtze River received the message and rushed to help, and prevent bandits from attacking and looting. It is now reported that the Hankou branch has sent a ship to assist in the rescue. However, it is still not out of danger, and the extent of the damage to the ship is unknown.

Weather Report

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky along the Chinese coast would be overcast, with strong northwesterly to northeasterly seasonal winds. Between the Ogasawara Islands, Kyushu, and the southeast coast of Japan, the weather is deteriorating due to the northward movement of a hurricane, with violent cyclones. The center of the hurricane was located at noon today within 120 miles of the intersection of 26 degrees north latitude and 138 degrees east longitude, moving northward with unknown wind force. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city reached a maximum of 77.9 and a minimum of 53.6. On the same day last year, the maximum was 79.2 and the minimum was 66.9.

Letters to the Editor

Regarding your newspaper's report (October 8th), on page 14 of section four, entitled "Collision Between Yunlong and Yongyuan Steamers Causes Damage," the following is a statement to clarify the facts, which do not entirely align with the report. Our company's Yunlong steamer was, in fact, struck by the Yongyuan steamer because the other vessel was unfamiliar with the Yangtze River navigation rules and went off course. Had our ship not taken emergency measures, the danger would have been considerable. The blame rests entirely with the Yongyuan. After the incident, we sent a letter of inquiry and requested compensation, but the company refused to accept the letter, only noting on the letter that the responsibility was still to be determined by an impartial party. Later, the other party asked a friend to intercede several times, so negotiations have not yet proceeded. The report in your newspaper today, based solely on the one-sided account of the other party, without any on-site investigation, is, in our opinion, regrettable. We hope that you will promptly issue a correction to set the record straight. Sincerely, Heng'an Chengji Steamboat Co., Ltd., October 8th.

To the Esteemed Editor of Shenbao, Greetings. Having read your newspaper's report regarding the collision between our Yongyuan and Yunlong vessels, we find that the information presented is slightly inaccurate, likely due to a misunderstanding by your reporter. We hereby submit this letter to clarify the matter and request a correction. Yours respectfully, Yongyuan Steamboat Co., October 8th, Telegram Address: 5207.

To the Esteemed Editor of Shenbao, Greetings. Your newspaper's local news column on September 27th published a report regarding the death of a patrolman who was shot. The report stated that the wife of the deceased, Jiang Shang, claimed that her husband, Jiang Guohua, had previously served as a militiaman in Pudong. This is completely untrue. Our militia has never employed anyone named Jiang Guohua, and our management committee has records to verify this. The false claim by Jiang Shang is likely intended to mislead and harm our reputation. We are submitting this information to be published in the Letters to the Editor column to set the record straight. Respectfully, The Joint Militia of Yangsi District, Gaoqiao District, Yangjing District, Gaohang District, Luhang District, and Tangqiao District, Shanghai.

To the Esteemed Editor of Shenbao, Greetings. I was astonished to read your newspaper's report on the 7th regarding the increased tax on liquor licenses by various liquor industry groups. As the director of general affairs, I did not identify myself as a section chief to representatives of the tobacco and liquor industry regarding the license tax. At the time, I stated that we would follow the regulations of the Ministry, and those who were concealing their income would be dealt with according to the regulations. However, those who were in compliance would naturally continue to pay according to the old rates. The claim that I insisted on raising the license fee from two yuan to four yuan is a complete misunderstanding. There were more than ten of them, and I showed them the license documents, which they all reviewed. How could there be such unfounded claims? As for the autumn tax amount, there may have been some concealment in the past due to disagreements between the Ministry and the provincial government. If we do not investigate the business situation and make thorough adjustments, how can we maintain national revenue and prevent fraud? Therefore, we cannot cite this as a precedent, which is also a difficult position. The claims of threats and harsh levies are likely intended to damage our bureau's reputation and are based on hearsay. I am submitting this letter for clarification and hope that it will be published in the Letters to the Editor column to set the record straight. Respectfully, Sun Shaoqing, Chief of General Affairs, Shanghai Tobacco and Liquor License Tax Collection Sub-Bureau, October 8th.

Page 17

Free Talk

Aphorisms of Ma Xiangbo, a Nonagenarian

Poetry, Prose, and Wine

— Jing Ji

Here are some miscellaneous notes on poetry, prose, and wine.

(A) Poetry

Old Man Xiangbo said: Chinese poetry is passable when describing scenery, but inferior to the works of famous Greek and Latin authors when discussing principles. Han Changli's poems describing fire scenes are quite interesting, as he uses many words denoting "red light"! Jiang Shiquan's courage is truly admirable. In one of his poems on morning purchases, he openly writes about "the birth of the Lord" so many years ago, i.e., the Kangxi year. Because now we only use the so-called "Gregorian calendar"!

(B) Prose

Old Man Xiangbo said: Chinese literati should cultivate their attitudes more. Because they love to be praised, and if someone says something bad about them, they immediately abandon the self-deprecating attitude they showed when they were being praised! They even engage in literary disputes over disagreements, as can be seen in Zeng Wenzheng's collection of writings. After all, everyone has different views, so why argue back and forth? For example, today I look at flowers and say red is good, but tomorrow I look again and say green is good. Even one's own views change from morning to night! Do all the self-proclaimed literary giants have to bow down to me alone? I think such an attitude is unnecessary!

(C) Wine

Old Man Xiangbo often advised us to drink a little wine at meals, saying that it can help with poetic inspiration. Because the vague intoxication of wine is precisely what literature calls imaginative emotion, and he cited many stories of literary giants and poets as proof. Of course, he did not encourage excessive drinking!

Candied Hawthorns

— Tie An

Sights and Sounds of the Old Capital

The Northern Capital inherits Mongolian traditions and greatly enjoys dairy foods. The saying that Southerners who come to the North are not fond of dairy products has been around for a long time. Today, there are milk tea shops on the streets that specialize in selling these foods. The milk cakes they make have a sour and smelly taste, which Northerners consider a delicacy, but Southerners often wrinkle their noses at. This difference in food preferences between North and South has persisted for thousands of years and has not been reconciled. The Ming dynasty followed Yuan customs, and many of its foods were taken from beyond its borders. Chen Yuan's "Sights and Sounds of the Imperial City" states that during the Ming dynasty, the court gave officials a box of seven kinds of sweets for the Winter Solstice: one was pine nut hailixuan. Zheng Yiwei said that the character xuan is not found in various dictionaries, and he also does not know what hailixuan is, probably a Yuan term. Another anecdote in "Jie'an Rambling Notes" states that on the eighth day of the fourth month of the Ming dynasty, the court gave officials Buluojia to eat outside the Wu Gate. Buluojia is also a Yuan term, which some say is zongzi (rice dumplings) or the current term bobo, which seems closer. Bobo is a general term for wheat foods. As for Manchu foods that are still popular today, sachima is one. It is made with rock sugar, cream, and white flour, shaped like glutinous rice, baked in a lime wood oven, and then cut into squares, which are sweet and greasy to eat. Furong cake is similar to sachima, but with brown sugar on the surface, resembling furong (hibiscus). Both of these do not have the taste of milk or cheese and can be appreciated even by Southerners. However, I think the most inexpensive and delicious is candied hawthorns. They are made by skewering grapes, yams, haitang fruit, haws, walnuts, etc., on bamboo sticks and dipping them in rock sugar, which is sweet, crunchy, and cool. Eating them on winter nights can refresh the palate. In the North, winter is not warm without a blazing stove, so it is good to eat cool foods to moisten the heart and lungs. In the Northeast, people often eat watermelon, but in the capital, they often substitute fresh grapes, which are white, juicy, and cool, and even the poor can enjoy their taste.

Two Seasonal Foods

Osmanthus Chestnuts

— Hong Liu

Osmanthus chestnuts are produced in Changshu and Lushan. When eaten, they have the aroma of osmanthus, hence the name. One theory is that the original variety is now extinct, and those sold on the market today are all ding, so the aroma is far less pronounced. As for why the original variety became extinct, according to old tales, there was a gentleman who retired to his home. He sighed over the osmanthus chestnuts, considering them a rarity of the world. Moreover, their production was very small, and he feared that they would be presented to the imperial garden, leading to annual tributes and corvée labor, which the people could not bear. Therefore, he bought all the trees and cut them down to prevent future troubles. The original variety was thus lost. I saw a poem by Mr. Zong Ziwei a few years ago that also commemorated this event, which may be true. It is a pity that the famous variety has not been passed down!

Red Mushrooms and Mist Dance

Are delicacies of autumn, with an extremely delicious taste, but many are poisonous. In general, those with delicate colors that change color in sunlight or turn silver black are inedible. Gifting them to superiors for consumption has been the practice since the Song dynasty. Fang Weng's poem says, "Sealed small gift box of red mushrooms." Red mushrooms are also known as mushrooms. Mushrooms that are red in color are often poisonous, so did the Song people eat poisonous mushrooms without harm?

Family Dietary Hygiene Methods

— Cao Ji Kuai

Beware of Disease Entering Through the Mouth

As the saying goes, a hundred diseases enter through the mouth. Although this statement does not entirely conform to medical theory, many digestive disorders are actually induced by food. Here are some of the simplest family dietary hygiene methods to offer to the people. If they can be implemented, they may prevent diseases from taking shape. (1) Boil utensils. Tableware such as chopsticks, spoons, bowls, and plates should be washed clean and boiled in a pot for ten minutes before eating to kill any attached fungi.

(2) Cook food thoroughly. No matter what kind of food it is, it must be fully boiled to ensure that it is thoroughly cooked before eating. Otherwise, it is easy to cause problems, especially with meat. (Because it often contains parasites.) Therefore, all fried meat and raw fish, shrimp, and crabs should not be eaten.

(3) Cleanliness of the cook. Anyone who cooks food, whether male or female, should strictly adhere to cleanliness, such as washing clothes and aprons frequently, cutting fingernails regularly, and washing away dirt from the hands, to prevent bacteria from harboring there.

(4) Discard leftover food. All food should be cooked and eaten immediately. If there are leftovers, they must be thoroughly boiled before eating. If the leftover food has a bad smell, it is a sign of bacteria and should not be eaten even if it is boiled. Boiling can kill bacteria, but the toxins of dead bacteria may still be present and harmful. Therefore, Confucius said not to eat food with a bad color or smell, which also means discarding leftover food.

(5) Drive away flies. Flies are excellent vectors for spreading bacteria, and food is a good culture medium for bacteria. Therefore, if flies come into contact with food, it is inevitable that it will be contaminated. Because prevention is difficult, the best way is to find ways to drive them away.

Tofu Snack Recipe

— Jing Ru

Good Taste

Tofu is a common food in our country, and Westerners consider it to be one of the most nutritious. Everyone knows how to make it, so there is no need to repeat it. The following details only the methods of cooking.

(1) Tofu Pudding comes in sweet and savory varieties, and the method is very simple. The sweet one is made by adding sugar to tofu whey. It is best eaten in the morning. The savory one is made by removing the whey and adding soy sauce, and then adding a little sesame oil. It is very good for eating with rice. Or you can add a little mustard powder. (Southerners hate mustard like an enemy, probably because they hate its bad breath. But they don't know that eating a little is very good for hygiene, and it has the effect of preventing epidemics and dispelling phlegm. After eating, rinse your mouth with clean water, and then hold a pinch of tea leaves in your mouth, and the smell will disappear.)

(2) Scrambled Tofu First stir-fry shredded meat in a pot, add appropriate seasonings, and then stir-fry with tofu.

(3) Chicken Lung Tofu First chop the chicken lung, mix it evenly with egg white, then stir-fry it in a pot with sesame oil, add appropriate seasonings, and then stir-fry with chopped tofu. The taste is quite sweet and fragrant.

(4) Stewed Tofu First boil clear soup in a pot, add seasonings, and then add tofu, abalone slices, and matsutake mushrooms to the pot to cook together. The taste is extremely delicious. It is also good to stew it with chicken offal.

(5) Fried Tofu Squeeze out the water from the tofu, add oil to a pot and fry it. Use it in place of meat to make various vegetarian dishes, all of which are excellent. I once saw something called stinky tofu in Shanghai, which had a strange and unpleasant smell, but many people liked it. I found that the way it was made was very unhygienic. And the authorities did not ban it, even allowing it to be sold on the streets, which I do not understand. (End note)

Pine Flowers of Qiyun Mountain

— He Lianlu

Qiyun Mountain is located fifteen miles southwest of Qixian County, two hundred li east of Gansu Province. The mountain is lined with Southern temples and lush with pines and cypresses. Deer and leopards can be found, and it also produces good musk. It can be called one of the famous mountains in Longshang. Every early autumn, a plant grows that is about three inches tall, yellow in color, and shaped like coral. The locals call it pine flower. It is sold in Yuyi and is considered a top-quality fresh vegetable with an exceptionally delicious taste. I have asked general travelers, and they all say that it is rare in China and abroad. However, after it is separated from the soil, it should be cooked immediately. If it is left for two or three days, its taste will be lacking, and it will easily become infested with insects. It is a pity that it is produced in a remote area in the northwest, and few people know about it. If it could be brought to the sea, then we could try this northwestern delicacy.

Sampan Congee at Lychee Bay

— Zhang Yi

Guangdong Flavors

Recently, a type of so-called "Sampan Congee" has become popular in Shanghai's Guangdong food restaurants. To Shanghainese, this name may seem novel and inexplicable; even Guangdong people who have lived in Shanghai for a long time and have not returned to their hometowns may not fully understand it. I must first do a little explanatory work here: "Sampan" means small boat, equivalent to what Shanghainese call "sanban" and Hangzhou people call "hua zi." "Congee" is just congee, no need to explain. But why is congee prefixed with the name "sampan"? It turns out that this type of congee is similar to "Fish Congee" and "Zhuangyuan Congee," but the ingredients are added or subtracted differently, and the creators were a group of boat people in Guangzhou who cooked and sold it on their boats. Its taste is indeed more delicious than ordinary fish congee, hence the name. Examining the preparation of fish congee, the ingredients include fish slices, meat patties, pig liver, pig intestines (small intestines), eggs, "zheng cai" (a type of dried salted vegetable sold in Guangdong stores), fried dough sticks, coriander (Shanghainese call it cilantro), scallions, soy sauce, cooked peanut oil, and pepper. Sampan congee, however, omits the meaningless pig liver and pig intestines, replacing them with crunchy peanuts, shredded jellyfish, and shrimp roe. First, a "ren zi huo" (a large, nearly cylindrical earthenware pot) is used to cook the chicken and congee together, supposedly using two or three chickens per pot. When eating, the remaining ingredients are arranged in the bowl, and then the congee is poured over them. Coriander, scallions, pepper, shrimp roe, peanuts, and other ingredients are added after the congee. Sampan congee has less liquid than fish congee, and the chewable parts account for six or seven tenths of it. Peanuts, jellyfish, and shrimp roe are its defining features. The Lychee Bay area is the most famous for selling sampan congee.

The name Lychee Bay is fascinating, but in reality, it is far inferior to West Lake; Shanghai's "Wa Li Da" is somewhat similar. However, Lychee Bay has many large trees, the water is more turbid, there are many dilapidated buildings on both sides, the boats on the water are quite crowded, and there is a time of day when many pleasure boats come and go.

Guangzhou's upper class enjoys leisure, but there are not many places for water recreation in Guangzhou, so Lychee Bay has been favored and gained fame. In recent years, a small golf course has been built on the nearby shore, and sampan congee has become very popular.

Except for the very short "deep winter" in the south, every sunny Saturday and Sunday, or on holidays, the upper class would invite their lovers, hire a sampan, and float on the less than two-mile-long Lychee Bay.

The rental price of a sampan, including the labor of the rower, is only one or two dimes per hour. A bowl of sampan congee costs one dime; someone with my appetite can eat two bowls when not hungry, and three bowls when hungry.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Words

The Art of Getting Along in the World

— Lu Ding

Whether you are in the Garden of Eden, whether you are in the Kingdom of Happiness, even if you are a favorite of heaven, every dream is inevitably dominated by the real environment.

This means that when a person reaches a certain age and time, there will always be a day to contact society and a day to struggle with the environment. If you do not have the art of getting along in the world, the result will be failure. Many people see the art of getting along in the world as a difficult task, but the art of getting along in the world is by no means difficult. Even if it is difficult, you should not fear it.

On the contrary! Many people see the art of getting along in the world as an easy task, but the art of getting along in the world is not easy. Even if it is easy, you should not ignore it.

Originally, an art, at least, has its own value. Of course, the art of getting along in the world is particularly important and particularly close to us.

Please ask those who are promoted to official positions and those who become rich, how did they achieve it? I don't believe they rely solely on their own abilities. I also don't believe they rely solely on their own good fortune. I am afraid that the art of getting along in the world has the greatest power. If so, sisters and brothers are exceptions.

To put it simply, the art of getting along in the world has the following characteristics. First, be aware of current affairs and watch the wind. Don't blunder about. Second, have a thick skin, don't be afraid of embarrassment, and don't be afraid of being laughed at. Third, be able to boast and flatter. If not, you can also use deception or intimidation.

These are the lessons that should be taught to those who have received long-term training in the specialized school of the art of getting along in the world. It is not enough to achieve them without sophisticated skills and insidious intentions.

Work hard, put your heart into it, and let's all study this art of getting along in the world.

Science

Radium and its Applications

— Meng Fu

Radium (Ra), abbreviated as radium, is a chemical element. It was discovered by the French chemists Mr. and Mrs. Curie. This element has many unique properties and is extremely relevant to the progress of modern chemistry and medicine.

Radium is widely distributed in various minerals, seawater, and some spring waters, but the amount is very small. Radium itself does not have crude ore; it is extracted from uranium ore. Most of the radium now available is extracted from a type of uranium ore called pitchblende. There are several pitchblende mines in the Belgian Congo region of Africa. However, the extraction of radium is one of the most difficult and expensive in mineral extraction chemistry. It is said that according to ordinary procedures, to obtain one ounce of radium, it is necessary to process 350 to 400 tons of crude ore. Moreover, the extraction methods are kept absolutely secret by each factory.

Radium is a white metal with a melting point of approximately 7000°C. It is easily altered in the air. Its chemical properties are similar to those of its sibling (barium), but it has another unique property, namely radioactivity. This action is actually a result of countless uranium atoms internally active. Here are some noteworthy strange phenomena: (1) Radium can emit light on its own, and this light is not caused by any kind of chemical combination. Therefore, even if it is placed in a vacuum, it can still emit light. (2) Radium can generate heat on its own, and this is not caused by any kind of chemical combination. (3) Radium can turn air into an electrical conductor. (4) Radium can emit several types of radiation (radial rays). This radiation can pass through opaque materials, such as black paper, wooden boards, and metal sheets, and cause changes in photographic film, similar to X-rays. Based on the different abilities to penetrate metal sheets, this radiation can be divided into three types: alpha, beta, and gamma. Alpha is the most difficult to penetrate, and it has the effect of generating heat and turning air into an electrical conductor. Magnets can attract it and cause it to bend, and it clearly has positive electrical properties. Beta has greater penetrating power, and magnets can also bend it. Because the bending direction is opposite to that of alpha, it can be known that it has negative electrical properties. Gamma has the strongest penetrating power, and even iron sheets as thick as twelve inches can be penetrated. This radiation has the ability to cause changes in photographic film and turn air into an electrical conductor. However, it is not attracted by magnets, so this radiation is actually a type of wave action, not made of solid matter. (5) Radium can gradually change into various other substances. For example, if a small amount of air is passed over radium, this air will contain a radioactive gas. This gas was initially called radium emanation. Now scientists call it Neton.

Speaking of the application of radium, it lies in the treatment of what was previously called incurable cancer. Because cancer can only be treated with radium, there is simply no hope of recovery with other medicines. The method of treatment is to irradiate the cancerous area with the gamma radiation of radium. Then the cancer cells will gradually shrivel. If the cancer cells completely shrivel and die, then it will work. However, gamma radiation can also damage healthy tissues in the human body. Therefore, the application of radium must have surgical skills. Now there is a new method, which is to use radioactive gas, which is the previously mentioned Neton. Radium has no other important uses besides medical use. For example, it can be used as a self-luminous dye, such as on the hands of luminous watches, but it is not only too expensive, but also has substitutes. Thick metal photography can also be replaced by cheaper X-rays.

Finally, everyone should know that this radium is the most precious thing in the world. Initially, it was worth 300,000 gold dollars per ounce. Now, because more is produced, it is still worth 150,000 gold dollars per ounce. Of course, the reason why it is so expensive is nothing more than the scarcity of production and the difficulty of extraction. At the same time, the needs of the medical community are also a contributing factor. Although radium is expensive, it also has an advantage, that is, the loss of radiation is extremely small. Even after two thousand years, only half of the light intensity will be lost.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Improvement of the Family System

— Zong Wen

A Comparison of New and Old Families

The organization of the family is nothing more than two types: cohabitation system and separation system. The cohabitation system is the so-called old family, and the separation system is the so-called new family. Originally, almost everyone in China adopted the cohabitation system, as if it had become a custom from ancient times to the present. Thus, stories such as "Zhang Gong's Hundred Tolerances" and "Five Generations Under One Roof" have been passed down as good stories to this day. But is the old family really good? Or is the new family good? This is a question that is very worthy of research and discussion, and it is also a very important and urgent issue in society to be resolved.

The important principle of the old family is the so-called "cohabitation." Speaking of this, I am afraid that someone will ask me, "Aren't their fathers, brothers, spouses, sisters-in-law, etc. in the old family able to gather in one place, which is very happy?" Indeed, originally its disadvantage is gathering in one place. Why?

(1) Too many people are noisy, which easily leads to dependence. The reason why Chinese people have dependence is originally cultivated in the family. If the people are like this, how can the country not be like this?

(2) Ill feelings are easily generated among the members. From then on, the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law, and sisters-in-law in the family will be suspicious of each other, and there will never be peaceful days. Even if the head of the family is very good, and the rest of the people are also very good, nothing will happen, right? But these are just some false masks of smiling faces and disunited hearts. In fact, can the personalities of all the people in a family be the same? As the saying goes, "One mother gives birth to nine sons, and even the mother has more than ten hearts." It's really well said. I assert, "The military nature of our country is probably also cultivated by the old family."

(3) Individuality cannot be freely developed, and an independent spirit cannot be cultivated.

(4) It is extremely difficult for the head of the family to deal with the members of the family.

(5) Comparison and jealousy are common to all people. In cohabiting families, laziness is often caused by comparison and jealousy. Every disadvantage must have an advantage. What is its advantage? This is talking about the economic aspect. In cohabiting families, property is pooled, which can increase the productivity. In terms of consumption, the consumption rate of cohabitation is small. For external economy, such as national taxation and social donations, they are mostly based on the family as a unit, so it is more economical than separation. Doesn't this point show that the old family also has advantages?

The important principle of the new family is the so-called "separation." Its advantages are as follows:

(1) By implementing the separation system, dependence can have no way to occur.

(2) After separation, not only will the friendship between brothers and sisters-in-law deepen, but also the feelings for parents-in-law will not be reduced at all. Because after separation, everyone can do their own things and be responsible for their own affairs. All the pain of restraint and the disadvantages of submission can be eliminated from now on. Mutual love and mutual help can be generated from now on.

(3) Individuality can be freely developed, and an independent spirit can be cultivated.

(4) After separation, family management is easier.

(5) After separation, although the same comparison and jealousy exist, the result is enough to make everyone strive to struggle.

In short, the advantages of cohabitation are limited to the material aspect, while the advantages of separation include the spiritual aspect. If the spiritual aspect is already sound, even if the material aspect is slightly consumed, it can be remedied. Moreover, because of careful planning, it can be saved instead, so why not do it?

Looking at the above points of comparison, the question of whether the old family is good or the new family is good can also be easily solved.

Over Tea and Wine

Interesting Anecdotes Heard and Seen at Banquets

— Ya Shi

Giving Cigarette Butts as Gifts

At the end of last month, my friend Mr. × mentioned that his friend Mr. ×, who had just left school for a few days, had obtained the nice position of magistrate of × County in × Province. This was such a glorious thing! He was going to take office that day, and I still needed to congratulate him. But I felt lonely on the way alone, and I thought you could go with me. I wonder what your opinion is? When I heard this, I was really envious and agreed to go together.

On that day, I dressed up and went forward with my friend Mr. ×. Arriving outside the lane, a greeter came forward to welcome us and walked into the lane together. Upon entering the door, I saw that the room was decorated with red knots everywhere and was extremely lively. The congratulatory guests were all erudite scholars. Everyone chatted for a long time. We were seated at the table, and the dishes were all delicacies from land and sea. The deliciousness need not be mentioned.

Only on the table across from us, there were piles of silver shields, calligraphy and paintings, bird's nest, ginseng, and everything precious. However, there was a box (about six or seven inches square and about two inches high) with particularly brocaded covering, with an unusually striking color. It must contain something that money cannot buy (my ideal). But I don't know how many silver dollars the owner of this gift spent. At that time, the recipient (the new magistrate) also felt curious and hurriedly came forward to open the box to see what kind of valuable thing it was. Just as the box was opened, the host turned red in the face and ran back into the room like a tiger turning over a mountain. The guests at the table were all surprised and stopped their cups when they saw this.

One of them immediately stood up and said with a smile, "Everyone, don't be suspicious of that small flower box. It is my respectful gift. My younger brother and the magistrate are classmates and are known to be close friends. Because I know that his esteemed self loves to eat cigarette butts the most, when we were classmates many years ago, the cigarette butts left over by our classmates were all left for him to eat. He liked it very much. Even the cigarette butts that were stepped on on the ground, he would pick them up to eat. Therefore, I specially presented a box today to bring joy. Who knew that the magistrate now no longer likes this thing? I am really out of touch." When the guests heard this, they all giggled and laughed non-stop. After a long time, the banquet ended, and after drinking fragrant tea, everyone thanked each other and returned home.

Wang Yuxing Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 795 yuan, with interest on 600 yuan at a rate of 5% per annum from November 5, 1931, and interest on the remaining 195 yuan at a rate of 5% per annum from March 31, 1932, until the date of execution.
