▲ Melchers & Co. v. Feilong Automobile Company Goods Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the goods debt of 61 taels of silver, with interest on the delay at a rate of 5% per annum from March 15, 1932, until the date of execution. The remaining claims are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear four-fifths of the litigation costs, and the defendant shall bear one-fifth.

▲ Leng Yaoxuan v. Wan Yecheng Loan Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,000 yuan, with interest at a rate of 2% per annum from March 27, 1927, until the date of execution. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Tao Hailian v. Tao Wangshi Divorce Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Pai Lihuote v. Yu Xuezhou Profit Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Yisheng Soda Company v. Yuanji Wine Store Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 138.27 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Liu Xiang v. Li Donglin Debt Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Zheng Shoumei v. Zhengshi Eviction Case (Main Text): The defendant shall immediately vacate the premises. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. The plaintiff's application for provisional execution is dismissed.

▲ Chengda Foreign Firm v. Taihe Xieji Trademark Dispute Case (Main Text): Defendant Taihe Xieji shall pay the plaintiff the bill amount of 431 taels, 6 qian, and 5 fen. Defendant Qiu Hongfu shall be responsible for clearing and repaying the debt. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Lu Jicui v. Xing Botao Rent Exemption Case (Main Text): The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff 2,726 yuan. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Li A'liu v. Dai Jiesheng Severance Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Chen Xian v. Zhu Yongbao Embezzlement Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Taiwan Tobacco Company v. Wang Xudong Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,236 yuan, with interest at a rate of 5% per annum from July 18 of this year until the date of execution. The plaintiff's application for provisional execution is dismissed. The litigation costs, except for the portion related to the application, shall be borne by the plaintiff; the remainder shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Zhu Juji v. Zhang Nanqiu Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 2,000 yuan, with interest at a rate of 2% per annum from September 10, 1931, until the date of execution. The plaintiff's application for provisional execution is dismissed. The litigation costs, except for the portion related to the application, shall be borne by the plaintiff; the remainder shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Jinkangzhuang v. Xi Shaoqing et al. Debt Case (Main Text): If the property of the defendant Yu Fuchangzhuang is insufficient to repay the plaintiff's 2,080 taels, 0 qian, and 7.4 fen of silver, with interest at a rate of 7.5 hao per month from January 1 of this year until the date of full repayment, the defendants shall be jointly and severally liable for the repayment. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne jointly and severally by the defendants.

▲ Huizhong Silver Company, Sadali v. Yuankang Silk Fabric Store Mortgage Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 2,699 taels and 8 qian of silver, with interest at a rate of 5% per annum from the date of filing the lawsuit until the date of execution. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Zhang Chengxun v. Li Gengfu et al. Debt Case (Main Text): Defendant Li Gengfu shall repay the plaintiff 3,600 yuan, with interest at a rate of 1% per month from April 1, 1932, until the date of execution. If the principal and interest of 3,000 yuan cannot be repaid, Yang Fansheng shall be responsible for repaying it on behalf of Li Gengfu. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant Li Gengfu.

▲ Faluo Fuer v. Tongming Electrical Company Compensation Case (Main Text): The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff 218 yuan. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear eight-ninths of the litigation costs, and the defendant shall bear one-ninth.

▲ Chen Zufa v. Qian Ruisheng et al. Debt Case (Main Text): Qian Ruisheng shall repay the plaintiff 1,000 taels of silver, with interest at a rate of 1% per month from January 27 of this year until the date of repayment. If Qian Ruisheng cannot repay the debt, Zhou Yongyi shall repay it on his behalf. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by Qian Ruisheng.

▲ Su Mengzhen v. Mi Zhanmeng et al. Loan Case (Main Text): Defendant Mi Zhanmeng shall repay the plaintiff the loan of 150 yuan. If he fails to fulfill his obligations, defendant Jin Yushan shall repay the loan on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by defendant Mi Zhanmeng.

▲ Ye Guang Company, Baike v. Wuxing Rent Arrears Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 144 yuan. The litigation costs related to the defendant's being sued shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Aierde Company v. Kefen Tianfu Rent Arrears Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 490 taels and 7 yuan. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are dismissed. The defendant shall bear seven-tenths of the litigation costs, and the plaintiff shall bear three-tenths.

▲ Lizhen Heng v. Shao Yuanfa Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 98 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Chen Shuishi v. Chen A'fa Divorce Case (Main Text): The divorce of the two parties is approved. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Zhou Shi v. Li Laosan Loan Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the loan principal of 600 yuan and interest of 156 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Gan Shuheng et al. v. Gan Liushi et al. Confirmation of Rights Case (Main Text): It is confirmed that the defendants have no right to demand that the plaintiffs hand over the account books. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants.

▲ Li Zhangshi v. Li Cunyi Cohabitation Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim and her application for provisional execution are both dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Atesheng v. Wu Junqing Loan Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the loan of 200 yuan, to be paid in monthly installments of 20 yuan from October 1932 to July 1933. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Wang Yangshi v. Wang Dingfu Revocation of Gift Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's gift of real estate to the defendant is permitted to be revoked. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Ketai Xin v. Zhu Shaobai Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 60 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Hu Gengchang v. Huang Jinxiu et al. Execution Objection Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Cai Tonghao et al. v. Zhang Bingkui Embezzlement Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim and the defendant's counterclaim are both dismissed. The litigation costs shall be borne by each party.

▲ Liu Guangfa et al. v. Qian Youzeng Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiffs Liu Guangfa, Pan Lianyuan, Liu Shaofu, and Lü Changming 42 yuan each, and shall repay the plaintiff Fang Chongxue 63 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Xu Daoguang v. Ma Changshu et al. Debt Case (Main Text): Defendant Ma Changshu shall repay the plaintiff 1,000 yuan, with interest at a rate of 5% per annum from July 3, 1931, until the date of execution. Defendant Pan Linji shall repay the plaintiff 240 yuan, with interest on 140 yuan at a rate of 5% per annum from February 4, 1931, and interest on 100 yuan at a rate of 5% per annum from March 10 of the same year, both until the date of execution. Defendant Wang Guoliang shall repay the plaintiff 162 yuan, with interest on 100 yuan at a rate of 2% per annum from November 8, 1930, and interest on 62 yuan at a rate of 2% per annum from February 25, 1931, both until the date of execution. Defendant Gui Liang shall repay the plaintiff 220 yuan, with interest at a rate of 5% per annum from December 8, 1931, until the date of execution. Defendant Xu Haishan shall repay the plaintiff 400 yuan, with interest on 100 yuan at a rate of 2% per annum from February 27, 1930, interest on 100 yuan at a rate of 5% per annum from June 3 of the same year, and interest on 200 yuan at a rate of 5% per annum from June 11 of the same year, all until the date of execution. The litigation costs related to the defendant's being sued shall be borne by the defendants in proportion. (Above, October 8th)

▲ Criminal Judgment ▲ The Police Department sues Yan Meilong et al. for an opium case (Main Text) Yan Meilong is sentenced to six months imprisonment and a fine of forty yuan for the crime of providing his premises for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit. Zhong Qingxiang, also known as Zhong Asi, is sentenced to four months imprisonment and a fine of twenty yuan for the crime of assisting in providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit as a repeat offender. Xu Dehong, Su A'er, Lu Liansheng, Bai Ren, Zhou Lianqing, Zhou Asong, and Shen Shaolin are each sentenced to one month imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium substitutes. Zhu Ronglin and Zhou Ronglin are each sentenced to two months imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium substitutes as repeat offenders. If the fines are converted to imprisonment, two yuan shall be calculated as one day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be calculated as two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. Xu Dehong, Lu Liansheng, Bai Renjie, and Shen Shaolin are granted a two-year suspended sentence. The smoking paraphernalia and red pills are confiscated according to the list. ▲ The Police Department sues Zhang Shengshi et al. for an opium case (Main Text) Zhang Shengshi is sentenced to six months imprisonment for the crime of providing premises for others to smoke opium substitutes for profit. The smoking paraphernalia and red pills are confiscated according to the list. ▲ Criminal Judgment Judgment in the case of Zhu Chenshi for interfering with family affairs (Main Text) Zhu Chenshi is sentenced to eight months imprisonment for assisting in luring a man or woman under the age of twenty away from their parental authority for profit. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be calculated as two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. ▲ Judgment in the case of Dong Taochun for false accusation (Main Text) Dong Taochun is sentenced to two months imprisonment for the crime of false accusation. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be calculated as two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. ▲ Judgment in the case of Tang Ruzhong for interfering with family affairs (Main Text) Tang Ruzhong is sentenced to three years imprisonment for attempting to lure a man under the age of twenty. If the fine is not paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan shall be calculated as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be calculated as two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. Two bags of red pills, totaling twelve taels, are confiscated. ▲ Judgment in the case of Lu Ranchun, Qin Lirong, Zhang Yongsheng, Song Zhaogui, Zhu Meilin, Zhu A'er, Zhang A'er et al. for an opium case (Main Text) Lu Ranchun is sentenced to six months imprisonment and a fine of sixty yuan for providing his premises for others to smoke opium. Qin Lirong, Zhang Yongsheng, Song Zhaogui, Zhu Meilin, Zhu A'da, and Zhang A'er are each sentenced to one month imprisonment and a fine of fifteen yuan for smoking opium. If the fine is not paid after compulsory enforcement, one yuan shall be calculated as one day of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be calculated as two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. Five opium pipes, five opium lamps, one opium pipe, and three ashtrays with a small amount of ash are confiscated. (Above, October 7th)
